<pr_description>
[Feature]: Expose ask_user_questions through the packaged MCP server
## Summary
Expose ask_user_questions through @gsd-build/mcp-server so workflow MCP clients like Claude Code CLI can use structured user questions instead of failing compatibility checks.

## Problem to solve
The packaged MCP server already exposes the headless-safe workflow surface, but it still blocks guided flows that require ask_user_questions. That leaves the Claude Code CLI workflow transport unable to run interactive GSD units even when the client supports MCP elicitation. In local checkout flows, the spawned workflow server could also drift behind source changes because the transport preferred stale dist artifacts.

## Proposed solution
Add an MCP form-elicitation bridge for ask_user_questions in the packaged server, preserve the existing GSD answer JSON shape expected by prompts and write gates, add the tool to the workflow MCP compatibility surface, and make local workflow launches prefer live source modules and source CLI entrypoints when the TS resolve hook is available.

## Alternatives considered
Keeping ask_user_questions unavailable preserves a headless-only package surface, but that continues to block guided workflow units for elicitation-capable clients. Falling back to plain text prompts would bypass the structured answer contract GSD already depends on. Using form elicitation for secure_env_collect was also considered, but that would be the wrong security model for secrets.

## Use cases
- Running guided GSD milestone or slice discussions from Claude Code CLI over workflow MCP
- Allowing write-gated flows that depend on structured confirmation questions to proceed through the packaged server
- Keeping local checkout testing aligned with source changes instead of stale dist output during MCP workflow development

## Impact
Affected: users running GSD workflow MCP through Claude Code CLI or other elicitation-capable clients
Severity: medium
Frequency: whenever a guided workflow unit requires structured user input
Consequence: guided units fail capability checks or cannot collect the structured responses GSD expects

## Evidence or prior art
The in-process GSD extension already exposes ask_user_questions and existing prompts/write-gate logic expect its current JSON answer shape. The MCP SDK supports form elicitation, which is the appropriate transport for non-secret structured choices.

## Additional information
This change should keep secure_env_collect out of scope. That path should use MCP URL elicitation or another secure bridge rather than form elicitation.

</pr_description>

     1	/**
     2	 * Minimal tool interface matching GSD's AgentTool shape.
     3	 * Avoids a direct dependency on @gsd/pi-agent-core from this compiled module.
     4	 */
     5	export interface McpToolDef {
     6	  name: string
     7	  description: string
     8	  parameters: Record<string, unknown>
     9	  execute(
    10	    toolCallId: string,
    11	    params: Record<string, unknown>,
    12	    signal?: AbortSignal,
    13	    onUpdate?: unknown,
    14	  ): Promise<{
    15	    content: Array<{ type: string; text?: string; data?: string; mimeType?: string }>
    16	  }>
    17	}
    18	
    19	// MCP SDK subpath imports use wildcard exports (./*) that NodeNext resolves
    20	// at runtime but TypeScript cannot statically type-check. We construct the
    21	// specifiers dynamically so tsc treats them as `any`.
    22	// Use createRequire to resolve wildcard subpaths — CJS resolver auto-appends
    23	// .js, which the ESM wildcard export map does not (#3603).
    24	import { createRequire } from 'node:module'
    25	const _require = createRequire(import.meta.url)
    26	const MCP_PKG = '@modelcontextprotocol/sdk'
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * Starts a native MCP (Model Context Protocol) server over stdin/stdout.
    30	 *
    31	 * This enables GSD's tools (read, write, edit, bash, grep, glob, ls, etc.)
    32	 * to be used by external AI clients such as Claude Desktop, VS Code Copilot,
    33	 * and any MCP-compatible host.
    34	 *
    35	 * The server registers all tools from the agent session's tool registry and
    36	 * maps MCP tools/list and tools/call requests to GSD tool definitions and
    37	 * execution, respectively.
    38	 *
    39	 * All MCP SDK imports are dynamic to avoid subpath export resolution issues
    40	 * with TypeScript's NodeNext module resolution.
    41	 */
    42	export async function startMcpServer(options: {
    43	  tools: McpToolDef[]
    44	  version?: string
    45	}): Promise<void> {
    46	  const { tools, version = '0.0.0' } = options
    47	
    48	  const serverMod = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server`)
    49	  const stdioMod = await import(_require.resolve(`${MCP_PKG}/server/stdio`))
    50	  const typesMod = await import(_require.resolve(`${MCP_PKG}/types`))
    51	
    52	  const Server = serverMod.Server
    53	  const StdioServerTransport = stdioMod.StdioServerTransport
    54	  const { ListToolsRequestSchema, CallToolRequestSchema } = typesMod
    55	
    56	  // Build a lookup map for fast tool resolution on calls
    57	  const toolMap = new Map<string, McpToolDef>()
    58	  for (const tool of tools) {
    59	    toolMap.set(tool.name, tool)
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  const server = new Server(
    63	    { name: 'gsd', version },
    64	    { capabilities: { tools: {} } },
    65	  )
    66	
    67	  // tools/list — return every registered GSD tool with its JSON Schema parameters
    68	  server.setRequestHandler(ListToolsRequestSchema, async () => ({
    69	    tools: tools.map((t: McpToolDef) => ({
    70	      name: t.name,
    71	      description: t.description,
    72	      inputSchema: t.parameters,
    73	    })),
    74	  }))
    75	
    76	  // tools/call — execute the requested tool and return content blocks
    77	  server.setRequestHandler(CallToolRequestSchema, async (request: any) => {
    78	    const { name, arguments: args } = request.params
    79	    const tool = toolMap.get(name)
    80	    if (!tool) {
    81	      return {
    82	        isError: true,
    83	        content: [{ type: 'text' as const, text: `Unknown tool: ${name}` }],
    84	      }
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    try {
    88	      const result = await tool.execute(
    89	        `mcp-${Date.now()}`,
    90	        args ?? {},
    91	        undefined, // no AbortSignal
    92	        undefined, // no onUpdate callback
    93	      )
    94	
    95	      // Convert AgentToolResult content blocks to MCP content format
    96	      const content = result.content.map((block: any) => {
    97	        if (block.type === 'text') return { type: 'text' as const, text: block.text ?? '' }
    98	        if (block.type === 'image') return { type: 'image' as const, data: block.data ?? '', mimeType: block.mimeType ?? 'image/png' }
    99	        return { type: 'text' as const, text: JSON.stringify(block) }
   100	      })
   101	      return { content }
   102	    } catch (err: unknown) {
   103	      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)
   104	      return { isError: true, content: [{ type: 'text' as const, text: message }] }
   105	    }
   106	  })
   107	
   108	  // Connect to stdin/stdout transport
   109	  const transport = new StdioServerTransport()
   110	  await server.connect(transport)
   111	  process.stderr.write(`[gsd] MCP server started (v${version})\n`)
   112	}
   113

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/dist/mcp-server.js:
     1	// MCP SDK subpath imports use wildcard exports (./*) that NodeNext resolves
     2	// at runtime but TypeScript cannot statically type-check. We construct the
     3	// specifiers dynamically so tsc treats them as `any`.
     4	// Use createRequire to resolve wildcard subpaths — CJS resolver auto-appends
     5	// .js, which the ESM wildcard export map does not (#3603).
     6	import { createRequire } from 'node:module';
     7	const _require = createRequire(import.meta.url);
     8	const MCP_PKG = '@modelcontextprotocol/sdk';
     9	/**
    10	 * Starts a native MCP (Model Context Protocol) server over stdin/stdout.
    11	 *
    12	 * This enables GSD's tools (read, write, edit, bash, grep, glob, ls, etc.)
    13	 * to be used by external AI clients such as Claude Desktop, VS Code Copilot,
    14	 * and any MCP-compatible host.
    15	 *
    16	 * The server registers all tools from the agent session's tool registry and
    17	 * maps MCP tools/list and tools/call requests to GSD tool definitions and
    18	 * execution, respectively.
    19	 *
    20	 * All MCP SDK imports are dynamic to avoid subpath export resolution issues
    21	 * with TypeScript's NodeNext module resolution.
    22	 */
    23	export async function startMcpServer(options) {
    24	    const { tools, version = '0.0.0' } = options;
    25	    const serverMod = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server`);
    26	    const stdioMod = await import(_require.resolve(`${MCP_PKG}/server/stdio`));
    27	    const typesMod = await import(_require.resolve(`${MCP_PKG}/types`));
    28	    const Server = serverMod.Server;
    29	    const StdioServerTransport = stdioMod.StdioServerTransport;
    30	    const { ListToolsRequestSchema, CallToolRequestSchema } = typesMod;
    31	    // Build a lookup map for fast tool resolution on calls
    32	    const toolMap = new Map();
    33	    for (const tool of tools) {
    34	        toolMap.set(tool.name, tool);
    35	    }
    36	    const server = new Server({ name: 'gsd', version }, { capabilities: { tools: {} } });
    37	    // tools/list — return every registered GSD tool with its JSON Schema parameters
    38	    server.setRequestHandler(ListToolsRequestSchema, async () => ({
    39	        tools: tools.map((t) => ({
    40	            name: t.name,
    41	            description: t.description,
    42	            inputSchema: t.parameters,
    43	        })),
    44	    }));
    45	    // tools/call — execute the requested tool and return content blocks
    46	    server.setRequestHandler(CallToolRequestSchema, async (request) => {
    47	        const { name, arguments: args } = request.params;
    48	        const tool = toolMap.get(name);
    49	        if (!tool) {
    50	            return {
    51	                isError: true,
    52	                content: [{ type: 'text', text: `Unknown tool: ${name}` }],
    53	            };
    54	        }
    55	        try {
    56	            const result = await tool.execute(`mcp-${Date.now()}`, args ?? {}, undefined, // no AbortSignal
    57	            undefined);
    58	            // Convert AgentToolResult content blocks to MCP content format
    59	            const content = result.content.map((block) => {
    60	                if (block.type === 'text')
    61	                    return { type: 'text', text: block.text ?? '' };
    62	                if (block.type === 'image')
    63	                    return { type: 'image', data: block.data ?? '', mimeType: block.mimeType ?? 'image/png' };
    64	                return { type: 'text', text: JSON.stringify(block) };
    65	            });
    66	            return { content };
    67	        }
    68	        catch (err) {
    69	            const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
    70	            return { isError: true, content: [{ type: 'text', text: message }] };
    71	        }
    72	    });
    73	    // Connect to stdin/stdout transport
    74	    const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
    75	    await server.connect(transport);
    76	    process.stderr.write(`[gsd] MCP server started (v${version})\n`);
    77	}
    78

     1	/**
     2	 * Request User Input — LLM tool for asking the user questions
     3	 *
     4	 * Thin wrapper around the shared interview-ui. The LLM presents 1-3
     5	 * questions with 2-3 options each. Each question can be single-select (default)
     6	 * or multi-select (allowMultiple: true). A free-form "None of the above" option
     7	 * is added automatically to single-select questions.
     8	 *
     9	 * Based on: https://github.com/openai/codex (codex-rs/core/src/tools/handlers/ask_user_questions.rs)
    10	 */
    11	
    12	import type { ExtensionAPI } from "@gsd/pi-coding-agent";
    13	import { sanitizeError } from "./shared/sanitize.js";
    14	import { Text } from "@gsd/pi-tui";
    15	import { Type } from "@sinclair/typebox";
    16	import {
    17	        showInterviewRound,
    18	        type Question,
    19	        type QuestionOption,
    20	        type RoundResult,
    21	} from "./shared/tui.js";
    22	
    23	// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    24	
    25	interface LocalResultDetails {
    26	        remote?: false;
    27	        questions: Question[];
    28	        response: RoundResult | null;
    29	        cancelled: boolean;
    30	}
    31	
    32	interface RemoteResultDetails {
    33	        remote: true;
    34	        channel: string;
    35	        timed_out: boolean;
    36	        promptId?: string;
    37	        threadUrl?: string;
    38	        status?: string;
    39	        questions?: Question[];
    40	        response?: import("./remote-questions/types.js").RemoteAnswer;
    41	        error?: boolean;
    42	}
    43	
    44	type AskUserQuestionsDetails = LocalResultDetails | RemoteResultDetails;
    45	
    46	// ─── Schema ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    47	
    48	const OptionSchema = Type.Object({
    49	        label: Type.String({ description: "User-facing label (1-5 words)" }),
    50	        description: Type.String({ description: "One short sentence explaining impact/tradeoff if selected" }),
    51	});
    52	
    53	const QuestionSchema = Type.Object({
    54	        id: Type.String({ description: "Stable identifier for mapping answers (snake_case)" }),
    55	        header: Type.String({ description: "Short header label shown in the UI (12 or fewer chars)" }),
    56	        question: Type.String({ description: "Single-sentence prompt shown to the user" }),
    57	        options: Type.Array(OptionSchema, {
    58	                description:
    59	                        'Provide 2-3 mutually exclusive choices for single-select, or any number for multi-select. Put the recommended option first and suffix its label with "(Recommended)". Do not include an "Other" option for single-select; the client adds a free-form "None of the above" option automatically.',
    60	        }),
    61	        allowMultiple: Type.Optional(
    62	                Type.Boolean({
    63	                        description:
    64	                                "If true, the user can select multiple options using SPACE to toggle and ENTER to confirm. No 'None of the above' option is added. Default: false.",
    65	                }),
    66	        ),
    67	});
    68	
    69	const AskUserQuestionsParams = Type.Object({
    70	        questions: Type.Array(QuestionSchema, {
    71	                description: "Questions to show the user. Prefer 1 and do not exceed 3.",
    72	        }),
    73	});
    74	
    75	// ─── Per-turn deduplication ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    76	// Prevents duplicate question dispatches (especially to remote channels like
    77	// Discord) when the LLM calls ask_user_questions multiple times with the same
    78	// questions in a single turn. Keyed by full canonicalized payload (id, header,
    79	// question, options, allowMultiple) — not just IDs — so that calls with the
    80	// same IDs but different text/options are treated as distinct.
    81	
    82	import { createHash } from "node:crypto";
    83	
    84	interface CachedResult {
    85	        content: { type: "text"; text: string }[];
    86	        details: AskUserQuestionsDetails;
    87	}
    88	
    89	const turnCache = new Map<string, CachedResult>();
    90	
    91	/** @internal Exported for testing only. */
    92	export function questionSignature(questions: Question[]): string {
    93	        const canonical = questions
    94	                .map((q) => ({
    95	                        id: q.id,
    96	                        header: q.header,
    97	                        question: q.question,
    98	                        options: (q.options || []).map((o) => ({ label: o.label, description: o.description })),
    99	                        allowMultiple: !!q.allowMultiple,
   100	                }))
   101	                .sort((a, b) => a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
   102	        return createHash("sha256").update(JSON.stringify(canonical)).digest("hex").slice(0, 16);
   103	}
   104	
   105	/** Reset the dedup cache. Called on session boundaries. */
   106	export function resetAskUserQuestionsCache(): void {
   107	        turnCache.clear();
   108	}
   109	
   110	// ─── Race helper ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   111	
   112	interface RaceableResult {
   113	        content: { type: "text"; text: string }[];
   114	        details?: unknown;
   115	}
   116	
   117	/**
   118	 * Race a remote channel dispatch against the local TUI. The first to produce
   119	 * a valid (non-error, non-timeout) result wins. The loser is cancelled via
   120	 * the shared AbortController.
   121	 *
   122	 * If the local TUI responds first, the remote poll is aborted (the message
   123	 * stays in Discord/Slack but polling stops). If remote responds first, the
   124	 * local TUI prompt is cancelled.
   125	 *
   126	 * Returns null only when both sides fail or are cancelled.
   127	 */
   128	async function raceRemoteAndLocal(
   129	        startRemote: () => Promise<RaceableResult | null>,
   130	        startLocal: () => Promise<RoundResult | null | undefined>,
   131	        controller: AbortController,
   132	        questions: Question[],
   133	): Promise<RaceableResult | null> {
   134	        // Wrap local TUI result into the same shape as remote results
   135	        const localPromise = startLocal().then((result): RaceableResult | null => {
   136	                if (!result || Object.keys(result.answers).length === 0) return null;
   137	                return {
   138	                        content: [{ type: "text" as const, text: formatForLLM(result) }],
   139	                        details: { questions, response: result, cancelled: false } satisfies LocalResultDetails,
   140	                };
   141	        }).catch(() => null);
   142	
   143	        const remotePromise = startRemote().then((result): RaceableResult | null => {
   144	                if (!result) return null;
   145	                const details = result.details as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   146	                // Treat timeouts and errors as non-wins — let the local TUI win instead
   147	                if (details?.timed_out || details?.error) return null;
   148	                return result;
   149	        }).catch(() => null);
   150	
   151	        // Race: first non-null result wins
   152	        const winner = await Promise.race([
   153	                localPromise.then((r) => r ? { source: "local" as const, result: r } : null),
   154	                remotePromise.then((r) => r ? { source: "remote" as const, result: r } : null),
   155	        ]);
   156	
   157	        if (winner) {
   158	                // Cancel the loser
   159	                controller.abort();
   160	                return winner.result;
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        // First to resolve was null — wait for the other
   164	        const [localResult, remoteResult] = await Promise.all([localPromise, remotePromise]);
   165	        controller.abort();
   166	        return localResult ?? remoteResult;
   167	}
   168	
   169	// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   170	
   171	const OTHER_OPTION_LABEL = "None of the above";
   172	
   173	function errorResult(
   174	        message: string,
   175	        questions: Question[] = [],
   176	): { content: { type: "text"; text: string }[]; details: AskUserQuestionsDetails } {
   177	        return {
   178	                content: [{ type: "text", text: sanitizeError(message) }],
   179	                details: { questions, response: null, cancelled: true },
   180	        };
   181	}
   182	
   183	/** Convert the shared RoundResult into the JSON the LLM expects. */
   184	function formatForLLM(result: RoundResult): string {
   185	        const answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> = {};
   186	        for (const [id, answer] of Object.entries(result.answers)) {
   187	                const list: string[] = [];
   188	                if (Array.isArray(answer.selected)) {
   189	                        list.push(...answer.selected);
   190	                } else {
   191	                        list.push(answer.selected);
   192	                }
   193	                if (answer.notes) {
   194	                        list.push(`user_note: ${answer.notes}`);
   195	                }
   196	                answers[id] = { answers: list };
   197	        }
   198	        return JSON.stringify({ answers });
   199	}
   200	
   201	// ─── Extension ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   202	
   203	export default function AskUserQuestions(pi: ExtensionAPI) {
   204	        pi.registerTool({
   205	                name: "ask_user_questions",
   206	                label: "Request User Input",
   207	                description:
   208	                        "Request user input for one to three short questions and wait for the response. Single-select questions have 2-3 mutually exclusive options with a free-form 'None of the above' added automatically. Multi-select questions (allowMultiple: true) let the user toggle multiple options with SPACE and confirm with ENTER.",
   209	                promptGuidelines: [
   210	                        "Use ask_user_questions when you need the user to choose between concrete alternatives before proceeding.",
   211	                        "Keep questions to 1 when possible; never exceed 3.",
   212	                        "For single-select: each question must have 2-3 options. Put the recommended option first with '(Recommended)' suffix. Do not include an 'Other' or 'None of the above' option - the client adds one automatically.",
   213	                        "For multi-select: set allowMultiple: true. The user can pick any number of options. No 'None of the above' is added.",
   214	                ],
   215	                parameters: AskUserQuestionsParams,
   216	
   217	                async execute(_toolCallId, params, signal, _onUpdate, ctx) {
   218	                        // ── Per-turn dedup: return cached result for identical question sets ──
   219	                        const sig = questionSignature(params.questions);
   220	                        const cached = turnCache.get(sig);
   221	                        if (cached) {
   222	                                return {
   223	                                        content: [{ type: "text" as const, text: cached.content[0].text + "\n(Returned cached answer — this question set was already asked this turn.)" }],
   224	                                        details: cached.details,
   225	                                };
   226	                        }
   227	
   228	                        // Validation
   229	                        if (params.questions.length === 0 || params.questions.length > 3) {
   230	                                return errorResult("Error: questions must contain 1-3 items", params.questions);
   231	                        }
   232	
   233	                        for (const q of params.questions) {
   234	                                if (!q.options || q.options.length === 0) {
   235	                                        return errorResult(
   236	                                                `Error: ask_user_questions requires non-empty options for every question (question "${q.id}" has none)`,
   237	                                                params.questions,
   238	                                        );
   239	                                }
   240	                        }
   241	
   242	                        // ── Routing: race remote + local, remote-only, or local-only ────────
   243	                        const { tryRemoteQuestions, isRemoteConfigured } = await import("./remote-questions/manager.js");
   244	                        const hasRemote = isRemoteConfigured();
   245	
   246	                        // Case 1: Both remote and local UI available — race them.
   247	                        // The first response wins; the loser is cancelled via AbortController.
   248	                        if (hasRemote && ctx.hasUI) {
   249	                                const raceController = new AbortController();
   250	                                // Merge the parent signal so external cancellation propagates.
   251	                                const onParentAbort = () => raceController.abort();
   252	                                signal?.addEventListener("abort", onParentAbort, { once: true });
   253	                                const raceSignal = raceController.signal;
   254	
   255	                                const raceResult = await raceRemoteAndLocal(
   256	                                        () => tryRemoteQuestions(params.questions, raceSignal),
   257	                                        () => showInterviewRound(params.questions, { signal: raceSignal }, ctx as any),
   258	                                        raceController,
   259	                                        params.questions,
   260	                                );
   261	
   262	                                signal?.removeEventListener("abort", onParentAbort);
   263	
   264	                                if (raceResult) {
   265	                                        const details = raceResult.details as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   266	                                        if (details && !details.timed_out && !details.error && !details.cancelled) {
   267	                                                turnCache.set(sig, raceResult as unknown as CachedResult);
   268	                                        }
   269	                                        return { ...raceResult, details: raceResult.details as unknown };
   270	                                }
   271	                                // Both sides failed/cancelled — fall through to error
   272	                                return errorResult("ask_user_questions: no response received from local UI or remote channel", params.questions);
   273	                        }
   274	
   275	                        // Case 2: Remote configured but no local UI (headless) — remote only.
   276	                        if (hasRemote && !ctx.hasUI) {
   277	                                const remoteResult = await tryRemoteQuestions(params.questions, signal);
   278	                                if (remoteResult) {
   279	                                        const remoteDetails = remoteResult.details as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   280	                                        if (remoteDetails && !remoteDetails.timed_out && !remoteDetails.error) {
   281	                                                turnCache.set(sig, remoteResult as unknown as CachedResult);
   282	                                        }
   283	                                        return { ...remoteResult, details: remoteResult.details as unknown };
   284	                                }
   285	                                return errorResult("Error: remote channel configured but returned no result", params.questions);
   286	                        }
   287	
   288	                        // Case 3: No remote — local UI only.
   289	                        if (!ctx.hasUI) {
   290	                                return errorResult("Error: UI not available (non-interactive mode)", params.questions);
   291	                        }
   292	
   293	                        // Delegate to shared interview UI
   294	                        const result = await showInterviewRound(params.questions, {}, ctx as any);
   295	
   296	                        // RPC mode fallback: custom() returns undefined, so showInterviewRound
   297	                        // may return undefined. Fall back to sequential ctx.ui.select() calls.
   298	                        if (!result) {
   299	                                const answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> = {};
   300	                                for (const q of params.questions) {
   301	                                        const options = q.options.map((o) => o.label);
   302	                                        if (!q.allowMultiple) {
   303	                                                options.push(OTHER_OPTION_LABEL);
   304	                                        }
   305	                                        const selected = await ctx.ui.select(
   306	                                                `${q.header}: ${q.question}`,
   307	                                                options,
   308	                                                { signal, ...(q.allowMultiple ? { allowMultiple: true } : {}) },
   309	                                        );
   310	                                        if (selected === undefined) {
   311	                                                return errorResult("ask_user_questions was cancelled", params.questions);
   312	                                        }
   313	
   314	                                        // When the user picks "None of the above" on a single-select
   315	                                        // question, prompt for a free-text explanation so they are not
   316	                                        // trapped in a re-asking loop (bug #2715).
   317	                                        let freeTextNote = "";
   318	                                        const selectedStr = Array.isArray(selected) ? selected[0] : selected;
   319	                                        if (!q.allowMultiple && selectedStr === OTHER_OPTION_LABEL) {
   320	                                                const note = await ctx.ui.input(
   321	                                                        `${q.header}: Please explain in your own words`,
   322	                                                        "Type your answer here…",
   323	                                                );
   324	                                                if (note) {
   325	                                                        freeTextNote = note;
   326	                                                }
   327	                                        }
   328	
   329	                                        const answerList = Array.isArray(selected) ? selected : [selected];
   330	                                        if (freeTextNote) {
   331	                                                answerList.push(`user_note: ${freeTextNote}`);
   332	                                        }
   333	                                        answers[q.id] = { answers: answerList };
   334	                                }
   335	                                const roundResult: RoundResult = {
   336	                                        endInterview: false,
   337	                                        answers: Object.fromEntries(
   338	                                                Object.entries(answers).map(([id, a]) => [
   339	                                                        id,
   340	                                                        { selected: a.answers.length === 1 ? a.answers[0] : a.answers, notes: "" },
   341	                                                ]),
   342	                                        ),
   343	                                };
   344	                                const fallbackResult = {
   345	                                        content: [{ type: "text" as const, text: JSON.stringify({ answers }) }],
   346	                                        details: {
   347	                                                questions: params.questions,
   348	                                                response: roundResult,
   349	                                                cancelled: false,
   350	                                        } satisfies LocalResultDetails,
   351	                                };
   352	                                turnCache.set(sig, fallbackResult);
   353	                                return fallbackResult;
   354	                        }
   355	
   356	                        // Check if cancelled (empty answers = user exited)
   357	                        const hasAnswers = Object.keys(result.answers).length > 0;
   358	                        if (!hasAnswers) {
   359	                                return {
   360	                                        content: [{ type: "text", text: "ask_user_questions was cancelled before receiving a response" }],
   361	                                        details: { questions: params.questions, response: null, cancelled: true } satisfies LocalResultDetails,
   362	                                };
   363	                        }
   364	
   365	                        const successResult = {
   366	                                content: [{ type: "text" as const, text: formatForLLM(result) }],
   367	                                details: { questions: params.questions, response: result, cancelled: false } satisfies LocalResultDetails,
   368	                        };
   369	                        turnCache.set(sig, successResult);
   370	                        return successResult;
   371	                },
   372	
   373	                // ─── Rendering ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   374	
   375	                renderCall(args, theme) {
   376	                        const qs = (args.questions as Question[]) || [];
   377	                        let text = theme.fg("toolTitle", theme.bold("ask_user_questions "));
   378	                        text += theme.fg("muted", `${qs.length} question${qs.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""}`);
   379	                        if (qs.length > 0) {

   381	                                text += theme.fg("dim", ` (${headers})`);
   382	                        }
   383	                        for (const q of qs) {

   388	                                        : [...(q.options || []).map((o: QuestionOption) => o.label), OTHER_OPTION_LABEL];
   389	                                const prefix = multiSel ? "☐" : "";
   390	                                const numbered = optLabels.map((l, i) => `${prefix}${i + 1}. ${l}`).join(", ");
   391	                                text += `\n  ${theme.fg("dim", numbered)}`;
   392	                        }
   393	                        return new Text(text, 0, 0);
   394	                },
   395

     2	 * MCP Server — registers GSD orchestration, project-state, and workflow tools.
     3	 *
     4	 * Session tools (6): gsd_execute, gsd_status, gsd_result, gsd_cancel, gsd_query, gsd_resolve_blocker
     5	 * Read-only tools (6): gsd_progress, gsd_roadmap, gsd_history, gsd_doctor, gsd_captures, gsd_knowledge
     6	 * Workflow tools (17): planning, replanning, completion, validation, reassessment, gate result, and milestone status tools

     8	 * Uses dynamic imports for @modelcontextprotocol/sdk because TS Node16
     9	 * cannot resolve the SDK's subpath exports statically (same pattern as
    10	 * src/mcp-server.ts in the main package).
    11	 */

    33	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    34	// Tool result helpers
    35	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    36	
    37	/** Wrap a JSON-serializable value as MCP tool content. */
    38	function jsonContent(data: unknown): { content: Array<{ type: 'text'; text: string }> } {
    39	  return { content: [{ type: 'text' as const, text: JSON.stringify(data, null, 2) }] };
    40	}
    41	
    42	/** Return an MCP error response. */
    43	function errorContent(message: string): { isError: true; content: Array<{ type: 'text'; text: string }> } {
    44	  return { isError: true, content: [{ type: 'text' as const, text: message }] };
    45	}
    46	
    47	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    48	// gsd_query filesystem reader
    49	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    50	
    51	async function readProjectState(projectDir: string, _query: string): Promise<Record<string, unknown>> {
    52	  const gsdDir = join(resolve(projectDir), '.gsd');
    53	  const result: Record<string, unknown> = { projectDir: resolve(projectDir) };
    54	
    55	  // STATE.md — current execution state
    56	  try {
    57	    result.state = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'STATE.md'), 'utf-8');
    58	  } catch {
    59	    result.state = null;
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  // PROJECT.md — project description
    63	  try {
    64	    result.project = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'PROJECT.md'), 'utf-8');
    65	  } catch {
    66	    result.project = null;
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  // REQUIREMENTS.md — requirement contract
    70	  try {
    71	    result.requirements = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'REQUIREMENTS.md'), 'utf-8');
    72	  } catch {
    73	    result.requirements = null;
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  // List milestones with basic metadata
    77	  const milestonesDir = join(gsdDir, 'milestones');
    78	  try {
    79	    const entries = await readdir(milestonesDir, { withFileTypes: true });
    80	    const milestones: Array<{ id: string; hasRoadmap: boolean; hasSummary: boolean }> = [];
    81	    for (const entry of entries) {
    82	      if (!entry.isDirectory()) continue;
    83	      const mDir = join(milestonesDir, entry.name);
    84	      const hasRoadmap = await fileExists(join(mDir, `${entry.name}-ROADMAP.md`));
    85	      const hasSummary = await fileExists(join(mDir, `${entry.name}-SUMMARY.md`));
    86	      milestones.push({ id: entry.name, hasRoadmap, hasSummary });
    87	    }
    88	    result.milestones = milestones;
    89	  } catch {
    90	    result.milestones = [];
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  return result;
    94	}
    95	
    96	async function fileExists(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
    97	  try {
    98	    await stat(path);
    99	    return true;
   100	  } catch {
   101	    return false;
   102	  }
   103	}

   105	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   106	// MCP Server type — minimal interface for the dynamically-imported McpServer
   107	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   108	
   109	interface McpServerInstance {
   110	  tool(name: string, description: string, params: Record<string, unknown>, handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>): unknown;
   111	  connect(transport: unknown): Promise<void>;
   112	  close(): Promise<void>;
   113	}
   114	
   115	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   116	// createMcpServer
   117	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   118	
   119	/**
   120	 * Create and configure an MCP server with session, read-only, and workflow tools.
   121	 *
   122	 * Returns the McpServer instance — call `connect(transport)` to start serving.
   123	 * Uses dynamic imports for the MCP SDK to avoid TS subpath resolution issues.
   124	 */
   125	export async function createMcpServer(sessionManager: SessionManager): Promise<{
   126	  server: McpServerInstance;
   127	}> {
   128	  // Dynamic import — same workaround as src/mcp-server.ts
   129	  const mcpMod = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server/mcp.js`);
   130	  const McpServer = mcpMod.McpServer;
   131	
   132	  const server: McpServerInstance = new McpServer(
   133	    { name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION },
   134	    { capabilities: { tools: {} } },
   135	  );
   136	
   137	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   138	  // gsd_execute — start a new GSD auto-mode session
   139	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   140	  server.tool(
   141	    'gsd_execute',
   142	    'Start a GSD auto-mode session for a project directory. Returns a sessionId for tracking.',
   143	    {
   144	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   145	      command: z.string().optional().describe('Command to send (default: "/gsd auto")'),
   146	      model: z.string().optional().describe('Model ID override'),
   147	      bare: z.boolean().optional().describe('Run in bare mode (skip user config)'),
   148	    },
   149	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   150	      const { projectDir, command, model, bare } = args as {
   151	        projectDir: string; command?: string; model?: string; bare?: boolean;
   152	      };
   153	      try {
   154	        const sessionId = await sessionManager.startSession(projectDir, { command, model, bare });
   155	        return jsonContent({ sessionId, status: 'started' });
   156	      } catch (err) {
   157	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   158	      }
   159	    },
   160	  );
   161	
   162	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   163	  // gsd_status — poll session status
   164	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   165	  server.tool(
   166	    'gsd_status',
   167	    'Get the current status of a GSD session including progress, recent events, and pending blockers.',
   168	    {
   169	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   170	    },
   171	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   172	      const { sessionId } = args as { sessionId: string };
   173	      try {
   174	        const session = sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
   175	        if (!session) return errorContent(`Session not found: ${sessionId}`);
   176	
   177	        const durationMs = Date.now() - session.startTime;
   178	        const toolCallCount = session.events.filter(
   179	          (e) => (e as Record<string, unknown>).type === 'tool_use' ||
   180	                 (e as Record<string, unknown>).type === 'tool_execution_start'
   181	        ).length;
   182	
   183	        return jsonContent({
   184	          status: session.status,
   185	          progress: {
   186	            eventCount: session.events.length,
   187	            toolCalls: toolCallCount,
   188	          },
   189	          recentEvents: session.events.slice(-10),
   190	          pendingBlocker: session.pendingBlocker
   191	            ? {
   192	                id: session.pendingBlocker.id,
   193	                method: session.pendingBlocker.method,
   194	                message: session.pendingBlocker.message,
   195	              }
   196	            : null,
   197	          cost: session.cost,
   198	          durationMs,
   199	        });
   200	      } catch (err) {
   201	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   202	      }
   203	    },
   204	  );
   205	
   206	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   207	  // gsd_result — get accumulated session result
   208	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   209	  server.tool(
   210	    'gsd_result',
   211	    'Get the result of a GSD session. Returns partial results if the session is still running.',
   212	    {
   213	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   214	    },
   215	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   216	      const { sessionId } = args as { sessionId: string };
   217	      try {
   218	        const result = sessionManager.getResult(sessionId);
   219	        return jsonContent(result);
   220	      } catch (err) {
   221	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   222	      }
   223	    },
   224	  );
   225	
   226	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   227	  // gsd_cancel — cancel a running session
   228	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   229	  server.tool(
   230	    'gsd_cancel',
   231	    'Cancel a running GSD session. Aborts the current operation and stops the process.',
   232	    {
   233	      sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   234	    },
   235	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   236	      const { sessionId } = args as { sessionId: string };
   237	      try {
   238	        await sessionManager.cancelSession(sessionId);
   239	        return jsonContent({ cancelled: true });
   240	      } catch (err) {
   241	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   242	      }
   243	    },
   244	  );
   245

   247	  // gsd_query — read project state from filesystem (no session needed)

   252	    {
   253	      projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   254	      query: z.string().describe('What to query (e.g. "status", "milestones", "requirements")'),
   255	    },
   256	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   257	      const { projectDir, query } = args as { projectDir: string; query: string };

   291	
   292	  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------

   301	    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   302	      const { projectDir } = args as { projectDir: string };
   303	      try {
   304	        return jsonContent(readProgress(projectDir));
   305	      } catch (err) {
   306	        return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   307	      }
   308	    },
   309	  );
   310

     1	#!/usr/bin/env node
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * @gsd-build/mcp-server CLI — stdio transport entry point.
     5	 *
     6	 * Connects the MCP server to stdin/stdout for use by Claude Code,
     7	 * Cursor, and other MCP-compatible clients.
     8	 */
     9	
    10	import { SessionManager } from './session-manager.js';
    11	import { createMcpServer } from './server.js';
    12	
    13	const MCP_PKG = '@modelcontextprotocol/sdk';
    14	
    15	async function main(): Promise<void> {
    16	  const sessionManager = new SessionManager();
    17	
    18	  // Create the configured MCP server with all 12 tools (6 session + 6 read-only)
    19	  const { server } = await createMcpServer(sessionManager);
    20	
    21	  // Dynamic import for StdioServerTransport (same TS subpath workaround)
    22	  const { StdioServerTransport } = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server/stdio.js`);
    23	  const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
    24	
    25	  // Cleanup handler — stop all sessions before exiting
    26	  let cleaningUp = false;
    27	  async function cleanup(): Promise<void> {
    28	    if (cleaningUp) return;
    29	    cleaningUp = true;
    30	    process.stderr.write('[gsd-mcp-server] Shutting down...\n');
    31	    try {
    32	      await sessionManager.cleanup();
    33	    } catch {
    34	      // swallow cleanup errors
    35	    }
    36	    try {
    37	      await server.close();
    38	    } catch {
    39	      // swallow close errors
    40	    }
    41	    process.exit(0);
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  process.on('SIGTERM', () => void cleanup());
    45	  process.on('SIGINT', () => void cleanup());
    46	
    47	  // Handle stdin end — MCP client disconnected
    48	  process.stdin.on('end', () => void cleanup());
    49	
    50	  // Connect and start serving
    51	  try {
    52	    await server.connect(transport);
    53	    process.stderr.write('[gsd-mcp-server] MCP server started on stdio\n');
    54	  } catch (err) {
    55	    process.stderr.write(
    56	      `[gsd-mcp-server] Fatal: failed to start — ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}\n`
    57	    );
    58	    await sessionManager.cleanup();
    59	    process.exit(1);
    60	  }
    61	}
    62	
    63	main().catch((err) => {
    64	  process.stderr.write(
    65	    `[gsd-mcp-server] Fatal: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}\n`
    66	  );
    67	  process.exit(1);
    68	});

   251	function getAllowedProjectRoot(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string | null {
   252	  const configuredRoot = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim();
   253	  return configuredRoot ? resolve(configuredRoot) : null;
   254	}
   255	
   256	function isWithinRoot(candidatePath: string, rootPath: string): boolean {
   257	  const rel = relative(rootPath, candidatePath);
   258	  return rel === "" || (!rel.startsWith("..") && !isAbsolute(rel));
   259	}
   260	
   261	function validateProjectDir(projectDir: string, env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string {
   262	  if (!isAbsolute(projectDir)) {
   263	    throw new Error(`projectDir must be an absolute path. Received: ${projectDir}`);
   264	  }
   265	
   266	  const resolvedProjectDir = resolve(projectDir);
   267	  const allowedRoot = getAllowedProjectRoot(env);
   268	  if (allowedRoot && !isWithinRoot(resolvedProjectDir, allowedRoot)) {
   269	    throw new Error(
   270	      `projectDir must stay within the configured workflow project root. Received: ${resolvedProjectDir}; allowed root: ${allowedRoot}`,
   271	    );
   272	  }
   273	
   274	  return resolvedProjectDir;
   275	}
   276	
   277	function parseToolArgs<T>(schema: z.ZodType<T>, args: Record<string, unknown>): T {
   278	  return schema.parse(args);
   279	}
   280	
   281	function parseWorkflowArgs<T extends { projectDir: string }>(
   282	  schema: z.ZodType<T>,
   283	  args: Record<string, unknown>,
   284	): T {
   285	  const parsed = parseToolArgs(schema, args);
   286	  return {
   287	    ...parsed,
   288	    projectDir: validateProjectDir(parsed.projectDir),
   289	  };
   290	}
   291	
   292	function isWorkflowToolExecutors(value: unknown): value is WorkflowToolExecutors {
   293	  if (!value || typeof value !== "object") return false;
   294	  const record = value as Record<string, unknown>;
   295	  const functionExports = [
   296	    "executeMilestoneStatus",
   297	    "executePlanMilestone",
   298	    "executePlanSlice",
   299	    "executeReplanSlice",
   300	    "executeSliceComplete",
   301	    "executeCompleteMilestone",
   302	    "executeValidateMilestone",
   303	    "executeReassessRoadmap",
   304	    "executeSaveGateResult",
   305	    "executeSummarySave",
   306	    "executeTaskComplete",
   307	  ];
   308	
   309	  return Array.isArray(record.SUPPORTED_SUMMARY_ARTIFACT_TYPES) &&
   310	    functionExports.every((key) => typeof record[key] === "function");
   311	}
   312	
   313	function getSupportedSummaryArtifactTypes(executors: WorkflowToolExecutors): readonly string[] {
   314	  return executors.SUPPORTED_SUMMARY_ARTIFACT_TYPES;
   315	}
   316	
   317	function getWriteGateModuleCandidates(): string[] {
   318	  const candidates: string[] = [];
   319	  const explicitModule = process.env.GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE?.trim();
   320	  if (explicitModule) {
   321	    if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(explicitModule) && !explicitModule.startsWith("file:")) {
   322	      throw new Error("GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE only supports file: URLs or filesystem paths.");
   323	    }
   324	    candidates.push(explicitModule.startsWith("file:") ? explicitModule : toFileUrl(explicitModule));
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  candidates.push(
   328	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url).href,
   329	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.ts", import.meta.url).href,
   330	  );
   331	
   332	  return [...new Set(candidates)];
   333	}
   334	
   335	function toFileUrl(modulePath: string): string {
   336	  return pathToFileURL(resolve(modulePath)).href;
   337	}
   338	
   339	function getWorkflowExecutorModuleCandidates(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env): string[] {
   340	  const candidates: string[] = [];
   341	  const explicitModule = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE?.trim();
   342	  if (explicitModule) {
   343	    if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(explicitModule) && !explicitModule.startsWith("file:")) {
   344	      throw new Error("GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE only supports file: URLs or filesystem paths.");
   345	    }
   346	    candidates.push(explicitModule.startsWith("file:") ? explicitModule : toFileUrl(explicitModule));
   347	  }
   348	
   349	  candidates.push(
   350	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.js", import.meta.url).href,
   351	    new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.ts", import.meta.url).href,
   352	  );
   353	
   354	  return [...new Set(candidates)];
   355	}
   356	
   357	async function getWorkflowToolExecutors(): Promise<WorkflowToolExecutors> {
   358	  if (!workflowToolExecutorsPromise) {
   359	    workflowToolExecutorsPromise = (async () => {
   360	      const attempts: string[] = [];
   361	      for (const candidate of getWorkflowExecutorModuleCandidates()) {
   362	        try {
   363	          const loaded = await import(candidate);
   364	          if (isWorkflowToolExecutors(loaded)) {
   365	            return loaded;
   366	          }
   367	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (module shape mismatch)`);
   368	        } catch (err) {
   369	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)})`);
   370	        }
   371	      }
   372	
   373	      throw new Error(
   374	        "Unable to load GSD workflow executor bridge for MCP mutation tools. " +
   375	        "Set GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE to an importable workflow-tool-executors module, " +
   376	        "or run the MCP server from a GSD checkout that includes src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.(js|ts). " +
   377	        `Attempts: ${attempts.join("; ")}`,
   378	      );
   379	    })();
   380	  }
   381	  return workflowToolExecutorsPromise;
   382	}
   383	
   384	async function getWorkflowWriteGateModule(): Promise<WorkflowWriteGateModule> {
   385	  if (!workflowWriteGatePromise) {
   386	    workflowWriteGatePromise = (async () => {
   387	      const attempts: string[] = [];
   388	      for (const candidate of getWriteGateModuleCandidates()) {
   389	        try {
   390	          const loaded = await import(candidate);
   391	          if (
   392	            loaded &&
   393	            typeof loaded.loadWriteGateSnapshot === "function" &&
   394	            typeof loaded.shouldBlockPendingGateInSnapshot === "function" &&
   395	            typeof loaded.shouldBlockQueueExecutionInSnapshot === "function"
   396	          ) {
   397	            return loaded as WorkflowWriteGateModule;
   398	          }
   399	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (module shape mismatch)`);
   400	        } catch (err) {
   401	          attempts.push(`${candidate} (${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)})`);
   402	        }
   403	      }
   404	
   405	      throw new Error(
   406	        "Unable to load GSD write-gate bridge for workflow MCP tools. " +
   407	        `Attempts: ${attempts.join("; ")}`,
   408	      );
   409	    })();
   410	  }
   411	  return workflowWriteGatePromise;
   412	}
   413	
   414	interface McpToolServer {
   415	  tool(
   416	    name: string,
   417	    description: string,
   418	    params: Record<string, unknown>,
   419	    handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>,
   420	  ): unknown;
   421	}
   422	
   423	async function runSerializedWorkflowOperation<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
   424	  // The shared DB adapter and workflow log base path are process-global, so
   425	  // workflow MCP mutations must not overlap within a single server process.
   426	  const prior = workflowExecutionQueue;
   427	  let release!: () => void;
   428	  workflowExecutionQueue = new Promise<void>((resolve) => {
   429	    release = resolve;
   430	  });
   431	
   432	  await prior;
   433	  try {
   434	    return await fn();
   435	  } finally {
   436	    release();
   437	  }
   438	}
   439	
   440	async function enforceWorkflowWriteGate(
   441	  toolName: string,
   442	  projectDir: string,
   443	  milestoneId: string | null = null,
   444	): Promise<void> {
   445	  const writeGate = await getWorkflowWriteGateModule();
   446	  const snapshot = writeGate.loadWriteGateSnapshot(projectDir);
   447	  const pendingGate = writeGate.shouldBlockPendingGateInSnapshot(
   448	    snapshot,
   449	    toolName,
   450	    milestoneId,
   451	    snapshot.activeQueuePhase,
   452	  );
   453	  if (pendingGate.block) {
   454	    throw new Error(pendingGate.reason ?? "workflow tool blocked by pending discussion gate");
   455	  }
   456	
   457	  const queueGuard = writeGate.shouldBlockQueueExecutionInSnapshot(
   458	    snapshot,
   459	    toolName,
   460	    "",
   461	    snapshot.activeQueuePhase,
   462	  );
   463	  if (queueGuard.block) {
   464	    throw new Error(queueGuard.reason ?? "workflow tool blocked during queue mode");
   465	  }
   466	}
   467

     1	/**
     2	 * Workflow MCP tools — exposes the core GSD mutation/read handlers over MCP.
     3	 */
     4	import { isAbsolute, relative, resolve } from "node:path";
     5	import { pathToFileURL } from "node:url";
     6	import { z } from "zod";
     7	let workflowToolExecutorsPromise = null;
     8	let workflowExecutionQueue = Promise.resolve();
     9	let workflowWriteGatePromise = null;
    10	function getAllowedProjectRoot(env = process.env) {
    11	    const configuredRoot = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim();
    12	    return configuredRoot ? resolve(configuredRoot) : null;
    13	}
    14	function isWithinRoot(candidatePath, rootPath) {
    15	    const rel = relative(rootPath, candidatePath);
    16	    return rel === "" || (!rel.startsWith("..") && !isAbsolute(rel));
    17	}
    18	function validateProjectDir(projectDir, env = process.env) {
    19	    if (!isAbsolute(projectDir)) {
    20	        throw new Error(`projectDir must be an absolute path. Received: ${projectDir}`);
    21	    }
    22	    const resolvedProjectDir = resolve(projectDir);
    23	    const allowedRoot = getAllowedProjectRoot(env);
    24	    if (allowedRoot && !isWithinRoot(resolvedProjectDir, allowedRoot)) {
    25	        throw new Error(`projectDir must stay within the configured workflow project root. Received: ${resolvedProjectDir}; allowed root: ${allowedRoot}`);
    26	    }
    27	    return resolvedProjectDir;
    28	}
    29	function parseToolArgs(schema, args) {
    30	    return schema.parse(args);
    31	}
    32	function parseWorkflowArgs(schema, args) {
    33	    const parsed = parseToolArgs(schema, args);
    34	    return {
    35	        ...parsed,
    36	        projectDir: validateProjectDir(parsed.projectDir),
    37	    };
    38	}
    39	function isWorkflowToolExecutors(value) {
    40	    if (!value || typeof value !== "object")
    41	        return false;
    42	    const record = value;
    43	    const functionExports = [
    44	        "executeMilestoneStatus",
    45	        "executePlanMilestone",
    46	        "executePlanSlice",
    47	        "executeReplanSlice",
    48	        "executeSliceComplete",
    49	        "executeCompleteMilestone",
    50	        "executeValidateMilestone",
    51	        "executeReassessRoadmap",
    52	        "executeSaveGateResult",
    53	        "executeSummarySave",
    54	        "executeTaskComplete",
    55	    ];
    56	    return Array.isArray(record.SUPPORTED_SUMMARY_ARTIFACT_TYPES) &&
    57	        functionExports.every((key) => typeof record[key] === "function");
    58	}
    59	function getSupportedSummaryArtifactTypes(executors) {
    60	    return executors.SUPPORTED_SUMMARY_ARTIFACT_TYPES;
    61	}
    62	function getWriteGateModuleCandidates() {
    63	    const candidates = [];
    64	    const explicitModule = process.env.GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE?.trim();
    65	    if (explicitModule) {
    66	        if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(explicitModule) && !explicitModule.startsWith("file:")) {
    67	            throw new Error("GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE only supports file: URLs or filesystem paths.");
    68	        }
    69	        candidates.push(explicitModule.startsWith("file:") ? explicitModule : toFileUrl(explicitModule));
    70	    }
    71	    candidates.push(new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url).href, new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.ts", import.meta.url).href);
    72	    return [...new Set(candidates)];
    73	}
    74	function toFileUrl(modulePath) {
    75	    return pathToFileURL(resolve(modulePath)).href;
    76	}
    77	function getWorkflowExecutorModuleCandidates(env = process.env) {
    78	    const candidates = [];
    79	    const explicitModule = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE?.trim();
    80	    if (explicitModule) {
    81	        if (/^[a-z]{2,}:/i.test(explicitModule) && !explicitModule.startsWith("file:")) {
    82	            throw new Error("GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE only supports file: URLs or filesystem paths.");
    83	        }
    84	        candidates.push(explicitModule.startsWith("file:") ? explicitModule : toFileUrl(explicitModule));
    85	    }
    86	    candidates.push(new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.js", import.meta.url).href, new URL("../../../src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.ts", import.meta.url).href);
    87	    return [...new Set(candidates)];
    88	}
    89	async function getWorkflowToolExecutors() {
    90	    if (!workflowToolExecutorsPromise) {
    91	        workflowToolExecutorsPromise = (async () => {
    92	            const attempts = [];
    93	            for (const candidate of getWorkflowExecutorModuleCandidates()) {
    94	                try {
    95	                    const loaded = await import(candidate);
    96	                    if (isWorkflowToolExecutors(loaded)) {
    97	                        return loaded;
    98	                    }
    99	                    attempts.push(`${candidate} (module shape mismatch)`);
   100	                }
   101	                catch (err) {
   102	                    attempts.push(`${candidate} (${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)})`);
   103	                }
   104	            }
   105	            throw new Error("Unable to load GSD workflow executor bridge for MCP mutation tools. " +
   106	                "Set GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE to an importable workflow-tool-executors module, " +
   107	                "or run the MCP server from a GSD checkout that includes src/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.(js|ts). " +
   108	                `Attempts: ${attempts.join("; ")}`);
   109	        })();
   110	    }
   111	    return workflowToolExecutorsPromise;
   112	}
   113	async function getWorkflowWriteGateModule() {
   114	    if (!workflowWriteGatePromise) {
   115	        workflowWriteGatePromise = (async () => {
   116	            const attempts = [];
   117	            for (const candidate of getWriteGateModuleCandidates()) {
   118	                try {
   119	                    const loaded = await import(candidate);
   120	                    if (loaded &&
   121	                        typeof loaded.loadWriteGateSnapshot === "function" &&
   122	                        typeof loaded.shouldBlockPendingGateInSnapshot === "function" &&
   123	                        typeof loaded.shouldBlockQueueExecutionInSnapshot === "function") {
   124	                        return loaded;
   125	                    }
   126	                    attempts.push(`${candidate} (module shape mismatch)`);
   127	                }
   128	                catch (err) {
   129	                    attempts.push(`${candidate} (${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)})`);
   130	                }
   131	            }
   132	            throw new Error("Unable to load GSD write-gate bridge for workflow MCP tools. " +
   133	                `Attempts: ${attempts.join("; ")}`);
   134	        })();
   135	    }
   136	    return workflowWriteGatePromise;
   137	}
   138	async function runSerializedWorkflowOperation(fn) {
   139	    // The shared DB adapter and workflow log base path are process-global, so
   140	    // workflow MCP mutations must not overlap within a single server process.
   141	    const prior = workflowExecutionQueue;
   142	    let release;
   143	    workflowExecutionQueue = new Promise((resolve) => {
   144	        release = resolve;
   145	    });
   146	    await prior;
   147	    try {
   148	        return await fn();
   149	    }
   150	    finally {
   151	        release();
   152	    }
   153	}
   154	async function enforceWorkflowWriteGate(toolName, projectDir, milestoneId = null) {
   155	    const writeGate = await getWorkflowWriteGateModule();
   156	    const snapshot = writeGate.loadWriteGateSnapshot(projectDir);
   157	    const pendingGate = writeGate.shouldBlockPendingGateInSnapshot(snapshot, toolName, milestoneId, snapshot.activeQueuePhase);
   158	    if (pendingGate.block) {
   159	        throw new Error(pendingGate.reason ?? "workflow tool blocked by pending discussion gate");
   160	    }
   161	    const queueGuard = writeGate.shouldBlockQueueExecutionInSnapshot(snapshot, toolName, "", snapshot.activeQueuePhase);
   162	    if (queueGuard.block) {
   163	        throw new Error(queueGuard.reason ?? "workflow tool blocked during queue mode");
   164	    }
   165	}
   166	async function handleTaskComplete(projectDir, args) {
   167	    await enforceWorkflowWriteGate("gsd_task_complete", projectDir, args.milestoneId);
   168	    const { taskId, sliceId, milestoneId, oneLiner, narrative, verification, deviations, knownIssues, keyFiles, keyDecisions, blockerDiscovered, verificationEvidence, } = args;
   169	    const { executeTaskComplete } = await getWorkflowToolExecutors();
   170	    return runSerializedWorkflowOperation(() => executeTaskComplete({
   171	        taskId,
   172	        sliceId,
   173	        milestoneId,
   174	        oneLiner,
   175	        narrative,
   176	        verification,
   177	        deviations,
   178	        knownIssues,
   179	        keyFiles,
   180	        keyDecisions,
   181	        blockerDiscovered,
   182	        verificationEvidence,
   183	    }, projectDir));
   184	}
   185	async function handleSliceComplete(projectDir, args) {
   186	    await enforceWorkflowWriteGate("gsd_slice_complete", projectDir, args.milestoneId);
   187	    const { executeSliceComplete } = await getWorkflowToolExecutors();
   188	    const { projectDir: _projectDir, ...params } = args;
   189	    return runSerializedWorkflowOperation(() => executeSliceComplete(params, projectDir));
   190	}
   191	async function handleReplanSlice(projectDir, args) {
   192	    await enforceWorkflowWriteGate("gsd_replan_slice", projectDir, args.milestoneId);
   193	    const { executeReplanSlice } = await getWorkflowToolExecutors();

   196	}
   197	async function handleCompleteMilestone(projectDir, args) {

   203	async function handleValidateMilestone(projectDir, args) {

     1	/**
     2	 * Answer Injector — pre-supply answers to headless mode questions.
     3	 *
     4	 * Loads a JSON answer file and intercepts extension_ui_request events
     5	 * to automatically respond with pre-configured answers, bypassing the
     6	 * default auto-responder or supervised mode.
     7	 */
     8	
     9	import { readFileSync } from 'node:fs'
    10	import { serializeJsonLine } from '@gsd/pi-coding-agent'
    11	
    12	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    13	// Types
    14	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    15	
    16	export interface AnswerFile {
    17	  questions?: Record<string, string | string[]>
    18	  secrets?: Record<string, string>
    19	  defaults?: { strategy?: 'first_option' | 'cancel' }
    20	}
    21	
    22	interface QuestionMeta {
    23	  id: string
    24	  header: string
    25	  question: string
    26	  options: string[]
    27	  allowMultiple?: boolean
    28	}
    29	
    30	export interface AnswerInjectorStats {
    31	  questionsAnswered: number
    32	  questionsDefaulted: number
    33	  secretsProvided: number
    34	}
    35	
    36	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    37	// Answer File Loader
    38	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    39	
    40	export function loadAndValidateAnswerFile(path: string): AnswerFile {
    41	  const raw = readFileSync(path, 'utf-8')
    42	  let parsed: unknown
    43	  try {
    44	    parsed = JSON.parse(raw)
    45	  } catch {
    46	    throw new Error(`Invalid JSON in answer file: ${path}`)
    47	  }
    48	
    49	  if (typeof parsed !== 'object' || parsed === null || Array.isArray(parsed)) {
    50	    throw new Error('Answer file must be a JSON object')
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  const obj = parsed as Record<string, unknown>
    54	
    55	  if (obj.questions !== undefined) {
    56	    if (typeof obj.questions !== 'object' || obj.questions === null || Array.isArray(obj.questions)) {
    57	      throw new Error('Answer file "questions" must be an object')
    58	    }
    59	    const questions = obj.questions as Record<string, unknown>
    60	    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(questions)) {
    61	      if (typeof value === 'string') continue
    62	      if (Array.isArray(value) && value.every((v) => typeof v === 'string')) continue
    63	      throw new Error(`Answer file "questions.${key}" must be a string or string[]`)
    64	    }
    65	  }
    66	
    67	  if (obj.secrets !== undefined) {
    68	    if (typeof obj.secrets !== 'object' || obj.secrets === null || Array.isArray(obj.secrets)) {
    69	      throw new Error('Answer file "secrets" must be an object')
    70	    }
    71	    const secrets = obj.secrets as Record<string, unknown>
    72	    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(secrets)) {
    73	      if (typeof value !== 'string') {
    74	        throw new Error(`Answer file "secrets.${key}" must be a string`)
    75	      }
    76	    }
    77	  }
    78	
    79	  if (obj.defaults !== undefined) {
    80	    if (typeof obj.defaults !== 'object' || obj.defaults === null || Array.isArray(obj.defaults)) {
    81	      throw new Error('Answer file "defaults" must be an object')
    82	    }
    83	    const defaults = obj.defaults as Record<string, unknown>
    84	    if (defaults.strategy !== undefined) {
    85	      if (defaults.strategy !== 'first_option' && defaults.strategy !== 'cancel') {
    86	        throw new Error('Answer file "defaults.strategy" must be "first_option" or "cancel"')
    87	      }
    88	    }
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  return obj as unknown as AnswerFile
    92	}
    93	
    94	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    95	// Answer Injector
    96	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    97	
    98	interface DeferredEvent {
    99	  event: Record<string, unknown>
   100	  writeToStdin: (data: string) => void
   101	  timer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>
   102	}
   103	
   104	export class AnswerInjector {
   105	  private readonly answerFile: AnswerFile
   106	  private readonly questionMetaByTitle = new Map<string, QuestionMeta>()
   107	  private readonly deferredEvents = new Map<string, DeferredEvent>()
   108	  private readonly usedQuestionIds = new Set<string>()
   109	  private readonly usedSecretKeys = new Set<string>()
   110	  private readonly stats: AnswerInjectorStats = {
   111	    questionsAnswered: 0,
   112	    questionsDefaulted: 0,
   113	    secretsProvided: 0,
   114	  }
   115	
   116	  constructor(answerFile: AnswerFile) {
   117	    this.answerFile = answerFile
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  /**
   121	   * Observe every event for question metadata (tool_execution_start of ask_user_questions).
   122	   */
   123	  observeEvent(event: Record<string, unknown>): void {
   124	    if (event.type !== 'tool_execution_start' || event.toolName !== 'ask_user_questions') return
   125	
   126	    // Extract questions from event.input.questions or event.args?.questions
   127	    const input = (event.input ?? event.args) as Record<string, unknown> | undefined
   128	    const questions = (input?.questions) as Array<Record<string, unknown>> | undefined
   129	    if (!Array.isArray(questions)) return
   130	
   131	    for (const q of questions) {
   132	      const header = String(q.header ?? '')
   133	      const question = String(q.question ?? '')
   134	      const title = `${header}: ${question}`
   135	      const options = Array.isArray(q.options)
   136	        ? (q.options as Array<Record<string, unknown>>).map((o) => String(o.label ?? ''))
   137	        : []
   138	
   139	      this.questionMetaByTitle.set(title, {
   140	        id: String(q.id ?? ''),
   141	        header,
   142	        question,
   143	        options,
   144	        allowMultiple: !!q.allowMultiple,
   145	      })
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    // Process any deferred events that now have metadata
   149	    for (const [title, deferred] of Array.from(this.deferredEvents)) {
   150	      if (this.questionMetaByTitle.has(title)) {
   151	        clearTimeout(deferred.timer)
   152	        this.deferredEvents.delete(title)
   153	        this.processWithMeta(deferred.event, deferred.writeToStdin)
   154	      }
   155	    }
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  /**
   159	   * Try to handle an extension_ui_request with pre-supplied answers.
   160	   * Returns true if the event was handled (or deferred for async handling).
   161	   */
   162	  tryHandle(event: Record<string, unknown>, writeToStdin: (data: string) => void): boolean {
   163	    const method = String(event.method ?? '')
   164	
   165	    // Only handle 'select' — let auto-responder handle confirm, input, etc.
   166	    if (method !== 'select') return false
   167	
   168	    const title = String(event.title ?? '')
   169	    const meta = this.questionMetaByTitle.get(title)
   170	
   171	    if (meta) {
   172	      return this.processWithMeta(event, writeToStdin)
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    // No metadata yet (out-of-order) — defer and handle asynchronously
   176	    const strategy = this.answerFile.defaults?.strategy ?? 'first_option'
   177	    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
   178	      this.deferredEvents.delete(title)
   179	      this.stats.questionsDefaulted++
   180	
   181	      if (strategy === 'cancel') {
   182	        const response = { type: 'extension_ui_response', id: event.id, cancelled: true }
   183	        writeToStdin(serializeJsonLine(response))
   184	      } else {
   185	        // first_option — send first option as response
   186	        const options = event.options as string[] | undefined
   187	        const response = { type: 'extension_ui_response', id: event.id, value: options?.[0] ?? '' }
   188	        writeToStdin(serializeJsonLine(response))
   189	      }
   190	    }, 500)
   191	
   192	    this.deferredEvents.set(title, { event, writeToStdin, timer })
   193	    return true
   194	  }
   195	
   196	  /**
   197	   * Get secret environment variables to inject into the RPC child process.
   198	   */
   199	  getSecretEnvVars(): Record<string, string> {
   200	    return this.answerFile.secrets ?? {}
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  /**
   204	   * Get a copy of the current stats.
   205	   */
   206	  getStats(): AnswerInjectorStats {
   207	    return { ...this.stats }
   208	  }
   209	
   210	  /**
   211	   * Get warnings for unused question IDs and secret keys.
   212	   */
   213	  getUnusedWarnings(): string[] {
   214	    const warnings: string[] = []
   215	
   216	    if (this.answerFile.questions) {
   217	      for (const id of Object.keys(this.answerFile.questions)) {
   218	        if (!this.usedQuestionIds.has(id)) {
   219	          warnings.push(`[answers] Warning: question ID '${id}' was never matched`)
   220	        }
   221	      }
   222	    }
   223	
   224	    if (this.answerFile.secrets) {
   225	      for (const key of Object.keys(this.answerFile.secrets)) {
   226	        if (!this.usedSecretKeys.has(key)) {
   227	          warnings.push(`[answers] Warning: secret '${key}' was provided but never requested`)
   228	        }
   229	      }
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    return warnings
   233	  }
   234	
   235	  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   236	  // Private
   237	  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   238	
   239	  private processWithMeta(event: Record<string, unknown>, writeToStdin: (data: string) => void): boolean {
   240	    const title = String(event.title ?? '')
   241	    const meta = this.questionMetaByTitle.get(title)
   242	    if (!meta) return false
   243	
   244	    const answer = this.answerFile.questions?.[meta.id]
   245	    const eventOptions = event.options as string[] | undefined
   246	
   247	    if (answer !== undefined) {
   248	      if (meta.allowMultiple) {
   249	        // Multi-select: answer must be an array
   250	        const values = Array.isArray(answer) ? answer : [answer]
   251	        const valid = values.every((v) => eventOptions?.includes(v))
   252	        if (valid) {
   253	          const response = { type: 'extension_ui_response', id: event.id, values }
   254	          writeToStdin(serializeJsonLine(response))
   255	          this.usedQuestionIds.add(meta.id)
   256	          this.stats.questionsAnswered++
   257	          return true
   258	        }
   259	      } else {
   260	        // Single-select: answer must be a string in the options
   261	        const value = Array.isArray(answer) ? answer[0] : answer
   262	        if (eventOptions?.includes(value)) {
   263	          const response = { type: 'extension_ui_response', id: event.id, value }
   264	          writeToStdin(serializeJsonLine(response))
   265	          this.usedQuestionIds.add(meta.id)
   266	          this.stats.questionsAnswered++
   267	          return true
   268	        }
   269	      }
   270	    }
   271	
   272	    // Answer not found or not valid — apply default strategy
   273	    const strategy = this.answerFile.defaults?.strategy ?? 'first_option'
   274	    this.stats.questionsDefaulted++
   275	
   276	    if (strategy === 'cancel') {
   277	      const response = { type: 'extension_ui_response', id: event.id, cancelled: true }
   278	      writeToStdin(serializeJsonLine(response))
   279	      return true
   280	    }
   281	
   282	    // first_option: return false to let the auto-responder handle it
   283	    return false
   284	  }
   285	}
   286
