    45	// ─── ID Generation with Reservation ─────────────────────────────────────────
    46	/**
    47	 * Generate the next milestone ID, accounting for reserved IDs, and reserve it.
    48	 * Ensures any preview ID shown in the UI matches what `gsd_milestone_generate_id`
    49	 * will later return.
    50	 */
    51	function nextMilestoneIdReserved(existingIds, uniqueEnabled) {
    52	    const allIds = [...new Set([...existingIds, ...getReservedMilestoneIds()])];
    53	    const id = nextMilestoneId(allIds, uniqueEnabled);
    54	    reserveMilestoneId(id);
    55	    return id;
    56	}
    57	// ─── Commit Instruction Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    58	/** Build commit instruction for planning prompts. .gsd/ is managed externally and always gitignored. */
    59	function buildDocsCommitInstruction(_message) {
    60	    return "Do not commit planning artifacts — .gsd/ is managed externally.";
    61	}
    62	const pendingAutoStartMap = new Map();
    63	/**
    64	 * Backward-compat bridge: returns a mutable reference to the entry matching
    65	 * basePath, or the sole entry when only one session exists.
    66	 * Internal use only — external code should use the Map directly.
    67	 */
    68	function _getPendingAutoStart(basePath) {
    69	    if (basePath)
    70	        return pendingAutoStartMap.get(basePath) ?? null;
    71	    if (pendingAutoStartMap.size === 1)
    72	        return pendingAutoStartMap.values().next().value;
    73	    return null;
    74	}
    75	/**
    76	 * Store pending auto-start state for a project.
    77	 * Exported for testing (#2985).
    78	 */
    79	export function setPendingAutoStart(basePath, entry) {
    80	    pendingAutoStartMap.set(basePath, { createdAt: Date.now(), ...entry });
    81	}
    82	/**
    83	 * Clear pending auto-start state.
    84	 * If basePath is given, clears only that project.  Otherwise clears all.
    85	 * Exported for testing (#2985).
    86	 */
    87	export function clearPendingAutoStart(basePath) {
    88	    if (basePath) {
    89	        pendingAutoStartMap.delete(basePath);
    90	    }
    91	    else {
    92	        pendingAutoStartMap.clear();
    93	    }
    94	}
    95	/**
    96	 * Returns the milestoneId being discussed for the given project.
    97	 * When basePath is omitted and only one session is active, returns that
    98	 * session's milestoneId for backward compatibility.  Returns null when
    99	 * multiple sessions exist and basePath is not specified (#2985 Bug 4).
   100	 */
   101	export function getDiscussionMilestoneId(basePath) {
   102	    if (basePath) {
   103	        return pendingAutoStartMap.get(basePath)?.milestoneId ?? null;
   104	    }
   105	    // Backward compat: return the sole entry's milestoneId, or null if ambiguous
   106	    if (pendingAutoStartMap.size === 1) {
   107	        return pendingAutoStartMap.values().next().value.milestoneId;
   108	    }
   109	    return null;
   110	}
   111	/** Called from agent_end to check if auto-mode should start after discuss */
   112	export function checkAutoStartAfterDiscuss() {
   113	    const entry = _getPendingAutoStart();
   114	    if (!entry)
   115	        return false;
   116	    const { ctx, pi, basePath, milestoneId, step } = entry;
   117	    // Gate 1: Primary milestone must have CONTEXT.md or ROADMAP.md
   118	    // The "discuss" path creates CONTEXT.md; the "plan" path creates ROADMAP.md.
   119	    const contextFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "CONTEXT");
   120	    const roadmapFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "ROADMAP");
   121	    if (!contextFile && !roadmapFile)
   122	        return false; // neither artifact yet — keep waiting
   123	    // Gate 2: STATE.md must exist — written as the last step in the discuss
   124	    // output phase. This prevents auto-start from firing during Phase 3
   125	    // (sequential readiness gates for remaining milestones) in multi-milestone
   126	    // discussions, where M001-CONTEXT.md exists but M002/M003 haven't been
   127	    // processed yet.
   128	    const stateFile = resolveGsdRootFile(basePath, "STATE");
   129	    if (!stateFile)
   130	        return false; // discussion not finalized yet
   131	    // Gate 3: Multi-milestone completeness warning
   132	    // Parse PROJECT.md for milestone sequence, warn if any are missing context.
   133	    // Don't block — milestones can be intentionally queued without context.
   134	    const projectFile = resolveGsdRootFile(basePath, "PROJECT");
   135	    let projectIds = [];
   136	    if (projectFile) {
   137	        try {
   138	            const projectContent = readFileSync(projectFile, "utf-8");
   139	            projectIds = parseMilestoneSequenceFromProject(projectContent);
   140	            if (projectIds.length > 1) {
   141	                const missing = projectIds.filter(id => {
   142	                    const hasContext = !!resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, id, "CONTEXT");
   143	                    const hasDraft = !!resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, id, "CONTEXT-DRAFT");
   144	                    const hasDir = existsSync(join(gsdRoot(basePath), "milestones", id));
   145	                    return !hasContext && !hasDraft && !hasDir;
   146	                });
   147	                if (missing.length > 0) {
   148	                    ctx.ui.notify(`Multi-milestone validation: ${missing.join(", ")} not found in filesystem. ` +
   149	                        `Discussion may not have completed all readiness gates.`, "warning");
   150	                }
   151	            }
   152	        }
   153	        catch (e) {
   154	            logWarning("guided", `PROJECT.md parsing failed: ${e.message}`);
   155	        }
   156	    }
   157	    // Gate 4: Discussion manifest process verification (multi-milestone only)
   158	    // The LLM writes DISCUSSION-MANIFEST.json after each Phase 3 gate decision.
   159	    // When it exists, validate it before auto-starting. Project history alone is
   160	    // not a reliable signal for the current discussion mode.
   161	    const manifestPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "DISCUSSION-MANIFEST.json");
   162	    if (existsSync(manifestPath)) {
   163	        try {
   164	            const manifest = JSON.parse(readFileSync(manifestPath, "utf-8"));
   165	            const total = typeof manifest.total === "number" ? manifest.total : 0;
   166	            const completed = typeof manifest.gates_completed === "number" ? manifest.gates_completed : 0;
   167	            if (total > 1 && completed < total) {
   168	                // Discussion not complete — block auto-start until all gates are done
   169	                return false;
   170	            }
   171	            // Cross-check manifest milestones against PROJECT.md if available
   172	            if (projectIds.length > 0) {
   173	                const manifestIds = Object.keys(manifest.milestones ?? {});
   174	                const untracked = projectIds.filter(id => !manifestIds.includes(id));
   175	                if (untracked.length > 0) {
   176	                    ctx.ui.notify(`Discussion manifest missing gates for: ${untracked.join(", ")}`, "warning");
   177	                }
   178	            }
   179	        }
   180	        catch (e) {
   181	            logWarning("guided", `discussion manifest verification failed: ${e.message}`);
   182	        }
   183	    }
   184	    // Draft promotion cleanup: if a CONTEXT-DRAFT.md exists alongside the new
   185	    // CONTEXT.md, delete the draft — it's been consumed by the discussion.
   186	    try {
   187	        const draftFile = resolveMilestoneFile(basePath, milestoneId, "CONTEXT-DRAFT");
   188	        if (draftFile)
   189	            unlinkSync(draftFile);
   190	    }
   191	    catch (e) {
   192	        logWarning("guided", `CONTEXT-DRAFT.md unlink failed: ${e.message}`);
   193	    }
   194	    // Cleanup: remove discussion manifest after auto-start (only needed during discussion)
   195	    try {
   196	        unlinkSync(manifestPath);
   197	    }
   198	    catch (e) {
   199	        logWarning("guided", `manifest unlink failed: ${e.message}`);
   200	    }
   201	    pendingAutoStartMap.delete(basePath);
   202	    ctx.ui.notify(`Milestone ${milestoneId} ready.`, "info");
   203	    startAuto(ctx, pi, basePath, false, { step }).catch((err) => {
   204	        ctx.ui.notify(`Auto-start failed: ${getErrorMessage(err)}`, "error");
   205	        logWarning("guided", `auto start error: ${getErrorMessage(err)}`);
   206	        debugLog("auto-start-failed", { error: getErrorMessage(err) });
   207	    });
   208	    return true;
   209	}
   210	/**
   211	 * Extract milestone IDs from PROJECT.md milestone sequence table.
   212	 * Looks for rows like "| M001 | Name | Status |" and extracts the ID column.
   213	 */
   214	function parseMilestoneSequenceFromProject(content) {
   215	    const ids = [];
   216	    const lines = content.split(/\r?\n/);
   217	    for (const line of lines) {
   218	        const match = line.match(/^\|\s*(M\d{3}[A-Z0-9-]*)\s*\|/);
   219	        if (match)
   220	            ids.push(match[1]);
   221	    }
   222	    return ids;
   223	}
   224	// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   225	/**
   226	 * Read GSD-WORKFLOW.md and dispatch it to the LLM with a contextual note.
   227	 * This is the only way the wizard triggers work — everything else is the LLM's job.
   228	 *
   229	 * When a unitType is provided, resolves the user's model preference for that
   230	 * phase (e.g., models.planning → "plan-milestone", models.discuss → "discuss-milestone") and applies it before
   231	 * dispatching. This ensures guided-flow dispatches respect the same
   232	 * per-phase model preferences that auto-mode uses.
   233	 */
   234	async function dispatchWorkflow(pi, note, customType = "gsd-run", ctx, unitType) {
   235	    // Route through the dynamic routing pipeline (complexity classification,
   236	    // tier downgrade, fallback chains) — same path as auto-mode dispatches (#2958).
   237	    if (ctx && unitType) {
   238	        const prefs = loadEffectiveGSDPreferences()?.preferences;
   239	        const result = await selectAndApplyModel(ctx, pi, unitType, /* unitId */ "", /* basePath */ process.cwd(), prefs, /* verbose */ false, /* autoModeStartModel */ null);
   240	        if (result.appliedModel) {
   241	            debugLog("guided-flow-model-applied", {
   242	                unitType,
   243	                model: `${result.appliedModel.provider}/${result.appliedModel.id}`,
   244	                routing: result.routing,
   245	            });
   246	        }
   247	        const compatibilityError = getWorkflowTransportSupportError(result.appliedModel?.provider ?? ctx.model?.provider, getRequiredWorkflowToolsForGuidedUnit(unitType), {
   248	            projectRoot: process.cwd(),
   249	            surface: "guided flow",
   250	            unitType,
   251	            authMode: result.appliedModel?.provider
   252	                ? ctx.modelRegistry.getProviderAuthMode(result.appliedModel.provider)
   253	                : ctx.model?.provider
   254	                    ? ctx.modelRegistry.getProviderAuthMode(ctx.model.provider)
   255	                    : undefined,
   256	            baseUrl: result.appliedModel?.baseUrl ?? ctx.model?.baseUrl,
   257	        });
   258	        if (compatibilityError) {
   259	            ctx.ui.notify(compatibilityError, "error");
   260	            return;
   261	        }
   262	    }
   263	    // Scope tools for discuss flows (#2949).
   264	    // Providers with grammar-based constrained decoding (xAI/Grok) return
   265	    // "Grammar is too complex" when the combined tool schema is too large.
   266	    // Discuss flows only need a small subset of GSD tools — strip the heavy
   267	    // planning/execution/completion tools to keep the grammar within limits.
   268	    let savedTools = null;
   269	    if (unitType?.startsWith("discuss-")) {
   270	        const currentTools = pi.getActiveTools();
   271	        savedTools = currentTools;
   272	        // Keep all non-GSD tools (builtins, other extensions) and only the
   273	        // GSD tools on the discuss allowlist.
   274	        const scopedTools = currentTools.filter((t) => !t.startsWith("gsd_") || DISCUSS_TOOLS_ALLOWLIST.includes(t));
   275	        pi.setActiveTools(scopedTools);
   276	        debugLog("discuss-tool-scoping", {
   277	            unitType,
   278	            before: currentTools.length,
   279	            after: scopedTools.length,
   280	            removed: currentTools.length - scopedTools.length,
   281	        });
   282	    }
   283	    const workflowPath = process.env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PATH ?? join(process.env.HOME ?? "~", ".gsd", "agent", "GSD-WORKFLOW.md");
   284	    const workflow = readFileSync(workflowPath, "utf-8");
   285	    pi.sendMessage({
   286	        customType,
   287	        content: `Read the following GSD workflow protocol and execute exactly.\n\n${workflow}\n\n## Your Task\n\n${note}`,
   288	        display: false,
   289	    }, { triggerTurn: true });
   290	    // Restore full tool set after the message is queued. The LLM turn has
   291	    // already captured the scoped set — restoring prevents the narrowed
   292	    // tools from leaking into subsequent dispatches (#3628).
   293	    if (savedTools) {
   294	        pi.setActiveTools(savedTools);
   295	    }
   296	}
   297	/**
   298	 * Resolve a model ID string to a model object from available models.
   299	 * Handles "provider/model" and bare ID formats.
   300	 */
   301	function resolveAvailableModel(modelId, availableModels, currentProvider) {
   302	    const slashIdx = modelId.indexOf("/");
   303	    if (slashIdx !== -1) {
   304	        const maybeProvider = modelId.substring(0, slashIdx);
   305	        const id = modelId.substring(slashIdx + 1);
   306	        const knownProviders = new Set(availableModels.map(m => m.provider.toLowerCase()));
   307	        if (knownProviders.has(maybeProvider.toLowerCase())) {
   308	            const match = availableModels.find(m => m.provider.toLowerCase() === maybeProvider.toLowerCase()
   309	                && m.id.toLowerCase() === id.toLowerCase());
   310	            if (match)
   311	                return match;
   312	        }
   313	        // Try matching the full string as a model ID (OpenRouter-style)
   314	        const lower = modelId.toLowerCase();
   315	        return availableModels.find(m => m.id.toLowerCase() === lower
   316	            || `${m.provider}/${m.id}`.toLowerCase() === lower);

    50	function parseJsonEnv<T>(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv, name: string): T | undefined {
    51	  const raw = env[name];
    52	  if (!raw) return undefined;
    53	  try {
    54	    return JSON.parse(raw) as T;
    55	  } catch {
    56	    throw new Error(`Invalid JSON in ${name}`);
    57	  }
    58	}
    59	
    60	function lookupCommand(command: string, platform: NodeJS.Platform = process.platform): string | null {
    61	  const lookup = platform === "win32" ? `where ${command}` : `which ${command}`;
    62	  try {
    63	    const resolved = parseLookupOutput(execSync(lookup, { timeout: 5_000, stdio: "pipe" }));
    64	    return resolved || null;
    65	  } catch {
    66	    return null;
    67	  }
    68	}
    69	
    70	function findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(startPath: string): string | null {
    71	  let current = resolve(startPath);
    72	
    73	  while (true) {
    74	    const candidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
    75	    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;
    76	
    77	    const parent = dirname(current);
    78	    if (parent === current) break;
    79	    current = parent;
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  return null;
    83	}
    84	
    85	function getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv): string | null {
    86	  const envAnchors = [
    87	    env.GSD_BIN_PATH?.trim(),
    88	    env.GSD_CLI_PATH?.trim(),
    89	    env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PATH?.trim(),
    90	  ].filter((value): value is string => typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0);
    91	
    92	  for (const anchor of envAnchors) {
    93	    const candidate = findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(anchor);
    94	    if (candidate) return candidate;
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  const candidates = [
    98	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url))),
    99	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url))),
   100	  ];
   101	
   102	  for (const bundledCli of candidates) {
   103	    if (existsSync(bundledCli)) return bundledCli;
   104	  }
   105	
   106	  return null;
   107	}
   108	
   109	function getBundledWorkflowExecutorModulePath(): string | null {
   110	  const candidates = [
   111	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../dist/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.js", import.meta.url))),
   112	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("./tools/workflow-tool-executors.js", import.meta.url))),
   113	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("./tools/workflow-tool-executors.ts", import.meta.url))),
   114	  ];
   115	
   116	  for (const candidate of candidates) {
   117	    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  return null;
   121	}
   122

   124	  const candidates = [
   125	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../dist/resources/extensions/gsd/bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url))),
   126	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("./bootstrap/write-gate.js", import.meta.url))),
   127	    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("./bootstrap/write-gate.ts", import.meta.url))),
   128	  ];

   131	    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;
   132	  }
   133	
   134	  return null;

   136	
   137	function buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(
   138	  projectRoot: string,
   139	  gsdCliPath: string | undefined,
   140	  explicitEnv?: Record<string, string>,
   141	): Record<string, string> {
   142	  const executorModulePath = getBundledWorkflowExecutorModulePath();
   143	  const writeGateModulePath = getBundledWorkflowWriteGateModulePath();
   144	
   145	  return {
   146	    ...(explicitEnv ?? {}),
   147	    ...(gsdCliPath ? { GSD_CLI_PATH: gsdCliPath } : {}),
   148	    ...(executorModulePath ? { GSD_WORKFLOW_EXECUTORS_MODULE: executorModulePath } : {}),
   149	    ...(writeGateModulePath ? { GSD_WORKFLOW_WRITE_GATE_MODULE: writeGateModulePath } : {}),
   150	    GSD_PERSIST_WRITE_GATE_STATE: "1",
   151	    GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT: projectRoot,
   152	  };
   153	}
   154	
   155	export function detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(
   156	  projectRoot = process.cwd(),
   157	  env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env,
   158	): WorkflowMcpLaunchConfig | null {
   159	  const name = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_NAME?.trim() || "gsd-workflow";
   160	  const explicitCommand = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_COMMAND?.trim();
   161	  const explicitArgs = parseJsonEnv<unknown>(env, "GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_ARGS");
   162	  const explicitEnv = parseJsonEnv<Record<string, string>>(env, "GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_ENV");
   163	  const explicitCwd = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_CWD?.trim();
   164	  const gsdCliPath = env.GSD_CLI_PATH?.trim() || env.GSD_BIN_PATH?.trim();
   165	  const workflowProjectRoot =
   166	    explicitEnv?.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   167	    env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   168	    env.GSD_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   169	    explicitCwd ||
   170	    projectRoot;
   171	  const resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot = resolve(workflowProjectRoot);
   172	
   173	  if (explicitCommand) {
   174	    const launchEnv = buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolve(workflowProjectRoot), gsdCliPath, explicitEnv);
   175	    return {
   176	      name,
   177	      command: explicitCommand,
   178	      args: Array.isArray(explicitArgs) && explicitArgs.length > 0 ? explicitArgs.map(String) : undefined,
   179	      cwd: explicitCwd || undefined,
   180	      env: Object.keys(launchEnv).length > 0 ? launchEnv : undefined,
   181	    };
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  const distCli = resolve(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
   185	  if (existsSync(distCli)) {
   186	    return {
   187	      name,
   188	      command: process.execPath,
   189	      args: [distCli],
   190	      cwd: resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot,
   191	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   192	    };
   193	  }
   194	
   195	  const bundledCli = getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env);
   196	  if (bundledCli) {
   197	    return {
   198	      name,
   199	      command: process.execPath,
   200	      args: [bundledCli],
   201	      cwd: resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot,
   202	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   203	    };
   204	  }
   205	
   206	  const binPath = lookupCommand("gsd-mcp-server");
   207	  if (binPath) {
   208	    return {
   209	      name,
   210	      command: binPath,
   211	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   212	    };
   213	  }
   214	
   215	  return null;
   216	}
   217	
   218	export function buildWorkflowMcpServers(
   219	  projectRoot = process.cwd(),
   220	  env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env,
   221	): Record<string, Record<string, unknown>> | undefined {
   222	  const launch = detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(projectRoot, env);
   223	  if (!launch) return undefined;
   224	
   225	  return {
   226	    [launch.name]: {
   227	      command: launch.command,
   228	      ...(launch.args && launch.args.length > 0 ? { args: launch.args } : {}),
   229	      ...(launch.env ? { env: launch.env } : {}),
   230	      ...(launch.cwd ? { cwd: launch.cwd } : {}),
   231	    },
   232	  };
   233	}

   235	export function getRequiredWorkflowToolsForGuidedUnit(unitType: string): string[] {
   236	  switch (unitType) {
   237	    case "discuss-milestone":
   238	      return ["gsd_summary_save", "gsd_plan_milestone"];
   239	    case "discuss-slice":
   240	      return ["gsd_summary_save"];
   241	    case "research-milestone":

   244	    case "plan-milestone":
   245	      return ["gsd_plan_milestone"];
   246	    case "plan-slice":
   247	      return ["gsd_plan_slice"];
   248	    case "execute-task":
   249	      return ["gsd_task_complete"];
   250	    case "complete-slice":
   251	      return ["gsd_slice_complete"];
   252	    default:
   253	      return [];
   254	  }

   290	export function usesWorkflowMcpTransport(
   291	  authMode: WorkflowCapabilityOptions["authMode"],
   292	  baseUrl: string | undefined,
   293	): boolean {
   294	  return authMode === "externalCli" && typeof baseUrl === "string" && baseUrl.startsWith("local://");
   295	}
   296	
   297	export function getWorkflowTransportSupportError(
   298	  provider: string | undefined,
   299	  requiredTools: string[],
   300	  options: WorkflowCapabilityOptions = {},
   301	): string | null {
   302	  if (!provider || requiredTools.length === 0) return null;
   303	  if (!usesWorkflowMcpTransport(options.authMode, options.baseUrl)) return null;
   304	
   305	  const projectRoot = options.projectRoot ?? process.cwd();
   306	  const env = options.env ?? process.env;
   307	  const launch = detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(projectRoot, env);
   308	  const surface = options.surface ?? "workflow dispatch";
   309	  const unitLabel = options.unitType ? ` for ${options.unitType}` : "";
   310	  const providerLabel = `"${provider}"`;
   311	
   312	  if (!launch) {
   313	    return `Provider ${providerLabel} cannot run ${surface}${unitLabel}: the GSD workflow MCP server is not configured or discoverable. Configure GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_COMMAND, build packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js, or install gsd-mcp-server on PATH.`;
   314	  }
   315	
   316	  const missing = [...new Set(requiredTools)].filter((tool) => !MCP_WORKFLOW_TOOL_SURFACE.has(tool));
   317	  if (missing.length === 0) return null;
   318	
   319	  return `Provider ${providerLabel} cannot run ${surface}${unitLabel}: this unit requires ${missing.join(", ")}, but the workflow MCP transport currently exposes only ${Array.from(MCP_WORKFLOW_TOOL_SURFACE).sort().join(", ")}.`;
   320	}

    32	function jsonContent(data) {
    33	    return { content: [{ type: 'text', text: JSON.stringify(data, null, 2) }] };

    39	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    40	// gsd_query filesystem reader
    41	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    42	async function readProjectState(projectDir, _query) {
    43	    const gsdDir = join(resolve(projectDir), '.gsd');
    44	    const result = { projectDir: resolve(projectDir) };
    45	    // STATE.md — current execution state
    46	    try {
    47	        result.state = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'STATE.md'), 'utf-8');
    48	    }
    49	    catch {
    50	        result.state = null;
    51	    }
    52	    // PROJECT.md — project description
    53	    try {
    54	        result.project = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'PROJECT.md'), 'utf-8');
    55	    }
    56	    catch {
    57	        result.project = null;
    58	    }
    59	    // REQUIREMENTS.md — requirement contract
    60	    try {
    61	        result.requirements = await readFile(join(gsdDir, 'REQUIREMENTS.md'), 'utf-8');
    62	    }
    63	    catch {
    64	        result.requirements = null;
    65	    }
    66	    // List milestones with basic metadata
    67	    const milestonesDir = join(gsdDir, 'milestones');
    68	    try {
    69	        const entries = await readdir(milestonesDir, { withFileTypes: true });
    70	        const milestones = [];
    71	        for (const entry of entries) {
    72	            if (!entry.isDirectory())
    73	                continue;
    74	            const mDir = join(milestonesDir, entry.name);
    75	            const hasRoadmap = await fileExists(join(mDir, `${entry.name}-ROADMAP.md`));
    76	            const hasSummary = await fileExists(join(mDir, `${entry.name}-SUMMARY.md`));
    77	            milestones.push({ id: entry.name, hasRoadmap, hasSummary });
    78	        }
    79	        result.milestones = milestones;
    80	    }
    81	    catch {
    82	        result.milestones = [];
    83	    }
    84	    return result;
    85	}
    86	async function fileExists(path) {
    87	    try {
    88	        await stat(path);
    89	        return true;
    90	    }
    91	    catch {
    92	        return false;
    93	    }
    94	}
    95	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    96	// createMcpServer
    97	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    98	/**
    99	 * Create and configure an MCP server with session, read-only, and workflow tools.
   100	 *
   101	 * Returns the McpServer instance — call `connect(transport)` to start serving.
   102	 * Uses dynamic imports for the MCP SDK to avoid TS subpath resolution issues.
   103	 */
   104	export async function createMcpServer(sessionManager) {
   105	    // Dynamic import — same workaround as src/mcp-server.ts
   106	    const mcpMod = await import(`${MCP_PKG}/server/mcp.js`);
   107	    const McpServer = mcpMod.McpServer;
   108	    const server = new McpServer({ name: SERVER_NAME, version: SERVER_VERSION }, { capabilities: { tools: {} } });
   109	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   110	    // gsd_execute — start a new GSD auto-mode session
   111	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   112	    server.tool('gsd_execute', 'Start a GSD auto-mode session for a project directory. Returns a sessionId for tracking.', {
   113	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   114	        command: z.string().optional().describe('Command to send (default: "/gsd auto")'),
   115	        model: z.string().optional().describe('Model ID override'),
   116	        bare: z.boolean().optional().describe('Run in bare mode (skip user config)'),
   117	    }, async (args) => {
   118	        const { projectDir, command, model, bare } = args;
   119	        try {
   120	            const sessionId = await sessionManager.startSession(projectDir, { command, model, bare });
   121	            return jsonContent({ sessionId, status: 'started' });
   122	        }
   123	        catch (err) {
   124	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   125	        }
   126	    });
   127	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   128	    // gsd_status — poll session status
   129	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   130	    server.tool('gsd_status', 'Get the current status of a GSD session including progress, recent events, and pending blockers.', {
   131	        sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   132	    }, async (args) => {
   133	        const { sessionId } = args;
   134	        try {
   135	            const session = sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
   136	            if (!session)
   137	                return errorContent(`Session not found: ${sessionId}`);
   138	            const durationMs = Date.now() - session.startTime;
   139	            const toolCallCount = session.events.filter((e) => e.type === 'tool_use' ||
   140	                e.type === 'tool_execution_start').length;
   141	            return jsonContent({
   142	                status: session.status,
   143	                progress: {
   144	                    eventCount: session.events.length,
   145	                    toolCalls: toolCallCount,
   146	                },
   147	                recentEvents: session.events.slice(-10),
   148	                pendingBlocker: session.pendingBlocker
   149	                    ? {
   150	                        id: session.pendingBlocker.id,
   151	                        method: session.pendingBlocker.method,
   152	                        message: session.pendingBlocker.message,
   153	                    }
   154	                    : null,
   155	                cost: session.cost,
   156	                durationMs,
   157	            });
   158	        }
   159	        catch (err) {
   160	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   161	        }
   162	    });
   163	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   164	    // gsd_result — get accumulated session result
   165	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   166	    server.tool('gsd_result', 'Get the result of a GSD session. Returns partial results if the session is still running.', {
   167	        sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   168	    }, async (args) => {
   169	        const { sessionId } = args;
   170	        try {
   171	            const result = sessionManager.getResult(sessionId);
   172	            return jsonContent(result);
   173	        }
   174	        catch (err) {
   175	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   176	        }
   177	    });
   178	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   179	    // gsd_cancel — cancel a running session
   180	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   181	    server.tool('gsd_cancel', 'Cancel a running GSD session. Aborts the current operation and stops the process.', {
   182	        sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   183	    }, async (args) => {
   184	        const { sessionId } = args;
   185	        try {
   186	            await sessionManager.cancelSession(sessionId);
   187	            return jsonContent({ cancelled: true });
   188	        }
   189	        catch (err) {
   190	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   191	        }
   192	    });
   193	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   194	    // gsd_query — read project state from filesystem (no session needed)
   195	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   196	    server.tool('gsd_query', 'Query GSD project state from the filesystem. Returns STATE.md, PROJECT.md, requirements, and milestone listing. Does not require an active session.', {
   197	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   198	        query: z.string().describe('What to query (e.g. "status", "milestones", "requirements")'),
   199	    }, async (args) => {
   200	        const { projectDir, query } = args;
   201	        try {
   202	            const state = await readProjectState(projectDir, query);
   203	            return jsonContent(state);
   204	        }
   205	        catch (err) {
   206	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   207	        }
   208	    });
   209	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   210	    // gsd_resolve_blocker — resolve a pending blocker
   211	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   212	    server.tool('gsd_resolve_blocker', 'Resolve a pending blocker in a GSD session by sending a response to the UI request.', {
   213	        sessionId: z.string().describe('Session ID returned from gsd_execute'),
   214	        response: z.string().describe('Response to send for the pending blocker'),
   215	    }, async (args) => {
   216	        const { sessionId, response } = args;
   217	        try {
   218	            await sessionManager.resolveBlocker(sessionId, response);
   219	            return jsonContent({ resolved: true });
   220	        }
   221	        catch (err) {
   222	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   223	        }
   224	    });
   225	    // =======================================================================
   226	    // READ-ONLY TOOLS — no session required, pure filesystem reads
   227	    // =======================================================================
   228	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   229	    // gsd_progress — structured project progress metrics
   230	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   231	    server.tool('gsd_progress', 'Get structured project progress: active milestone/slice/task, phase, completion counts, blockers, and next action. No session required — reads directly from .gsd/ on disk.', {
   232	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   233	    }, async (args) => {
   234	        const { projectDir } = args;
   235	        try {
   236	            return jsonContent(readProgress(projectDir));
   237	        }
   238	        catch (err) {
   239	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   240	        }
   241	    });
   242	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   243	    // gsd_roadmap — milestone/slice/task structure with status
   244	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   245	    server.tool('gsd_roadmap', 'Get the full project roadmap structure: milestones with their slices, tasks, status, risk, and dependencies. Optionally filter to a single milestone. No session required.', {
   246	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   247	        milestoneId: z.string().optional().describe('Filter to a specific milestone (e.g. "M001")'),
   248	    }, async (args) => {
   249	        const { projectDir, milestoneId } = args;
   250	        try {
   251	            return jsonContent(readRoadmap(projectDir, milestoneId));
   252	        }
   253	        catch (err) {
   254	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   255	        }
   256	    });
   257	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   258	    // gsd_history — execution history with cost/token metrics
   259	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   260	    server.tool('gsd_history', 'Get execution history with cost, token usage, model, and duration per unit. Returns totals across all units. No session required.', {
   261	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   262	        limit: z.number().optional().describe('Max entries to return (most recent first). Default: all.'),
   263	    }, async (args) => {
   264	        const { projectDir, limit } = args;
   265	        try {
   266	            return jsonContent(readHistory(projectDir, limit));
   267	        }
   268	        catch (err) {
   269	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   270	        }
   271	    });
   272	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   273	    // gsd_doctor — lightweight structural health check
   274	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   275	    server.tool('gsd_doctor', 'Run a lightweight structural health check on the .gsd/ directory. Checks for missing files, status inconsistencies, and orphaned state. No session required.', {
   276	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   277	        scope: z.string().optional().describe('Limit checks to a specific milestone (e.g. "M001")'),
   278	    }, async (args) => {
   279	        const { projectDir, scope } = args;
   280	        try {
   281	            return jsonContent(runDoctorLite(projectDir, scope));
   282	        }
   283	        catch (err) {
   284	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   285	        }
   286	    });
   287	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   288	    // gsd_captures — pending captures and ideas
   289	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   290	    server.tool('gsd_captures', 'Get captured ideas and thoughts from CAPTURES.md with triage status. Filter by pending, actionable, or all. No session required.', {
   291	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   292	        filter: z.enum(['all', 'pending', 'actionable']).optional().describe('Filter captures (default: "all")'),
   293	    }, async (args) => {
   294	        const { projectDir, filter } = args;
   295	        try {
   296	            return jsonContent(readCaptures(projectDir, filter ?? 'all'));
   297	        }
   298	        catch (err) {
   299	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   300	        }
   301	    });
   302	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   303	    // gsd_knowledge — project knowledge base
   304	    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   305	    server.tool('gsd_knowledge', 'Get the project knowledge base: rules, patterns, and lessons learned accumulated during development. No session required.', {
   306	        projectDir: z.string().describe('Absolute path to the project directory'),
   307	    }, async (args) => {
   308	        const { projectDir } = args;
   309	        try {
   310	            return jsonContent(readKnowledge(projectDir));
   311	        }
   312	        catch (err) {
   313	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   314	        }
   315	    });
   316	    registerWorkflowTools(server);
   317	    return { server };
   318	}
   319	//# sourceMappingURL=server.js.map

     2	 * @gsd-build/mcp-server — Integration and unit tests.
     3	 *
     4	 * Strategy: We cannot mock @gsd-build/rpc-client at the module level without
     5	 * --experimental-test-module-mocks. Instead we test by:
     6	 *

     8	 * 2. Testing event handling, state transitions, and error paths
     9	 * 3. Testing tool registration via createMcpServer
    10	 * 4. Testing CLI path resolution via static method

    23	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    24	// Mock RpcClient (duck-typed to match RpcClient interface)
    25	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    26	
    27	class MockRpcClient {
    28	  started = false;
    29	  stopped = false;
    30	  aborted = false;
    31	  prompted: string[] = [];
    32	  private eventListeners: Array<(event: Record<string, unknown>) => void> = [];
    33	  uiResponses: Array<{ requestId: string; response: Record<string, unknown> }> = [];
    34	
    35	  /** Control — set to make start() reject */
    36	  startError: Error | null = null;
    37	  /** Control — set to make init() reject */
    38	  initError: Error | null = null;
    39	  /** Control — override sessionId from init */
    40	  initSessionId = 'mock-session-001';
    41	
    42	  cwd: string;
    43	  args: string[];
    44	
    45	  constructor(options?: Record<string, unknown>) {
    46	    this.cwd = (options?.cwd as string) ?? '';
    47	    this.args = (options?.args as string[]) ?? [];
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  async start(): Promise<void> {
    51	    if (this.startError) throw this.startError;
    52	    this.started = true;
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  async stop(): Promise<void> {
    56	    this.stopped = true;
    57	  }
    58	
    59	  async init(): Promise<{ sessionId: string; version: string }> {
    60	    if (this.initError) throw this.initError;
    61	    return { sessionId: this.initSessionId, version: '2.51.0' };
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  onEvent(listener: (event: Record<string, unknown>) => void): () => void {
    65	    this.eventListeners.push(listener);
    66	    return () => {
    67	      const idx = this.eventListeners.indexOf(listener);
    68	      if (idx >= 0) this.eventListeners.splice(idx, 1);
    69	    };
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  async prompt(message: string): Promise<void> {
    73	    this.prompted.push(message);
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  async abort(): Promise<void> {
    77	    this.aborted = true;
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  sendUIResponse(requestId: string, response: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    81	    this.uiResponses.push({ requestId, response });
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  /** Test helper — emit an event to all listeners */
    85	  emitEvent(event: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    86	    for (const listener of this.eventListeners) {
    87	      listener(event);
    88	    }
    89	  }
    90	}

    92	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    93	// TestableSessionManager — injects mock clients without module mocking
    94	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    95	
    96	/**
    97	 * Subclass that overrides startSession to use MockRpcClient instead of the
    98	 * real RpcClient. We directly construct the session object, mirroring the
    99	 * parent's logic but with our mock.
   100	 */
   101	class TestableSessionManager extends SessionManager {
   102	  /** The last mock client created */
   103	  lastClient: MockRpcClient | null = null;
   104	  /** All mock clients */
   105	  allClients: MockRpcClient[] = [];
   106	  /** Counter for unique session IDs across multiple sessions */
   107	  private sessionCounter = 0;
   108	  /** Control: set to make startSession fail during init */
   109	  nextInitError: Error | null = null;
   110	  /** Control: set to make startSession fail during start */
   111	  nextStartError: Error | null = null;
   112	
   113	  override async startSession(projectDir: string, options: { cliPath?: string; command?: string; model?: string; bare?: boolean } = {}): Promise<string> {
   114	    if (!projectDir || projectDir.trim() === '') {
   115	      throw new Error('projectDir is required and cannot be empty');
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    const resolvedDir = resolve(projectDir);
   119	
   120	    // Check duplicate via getSessionByDir
   121	    const existing = this.getSessionByDir(resolvedDir);
   122	    if (existing) {
   123	      throw new Error(
   124	        `Session already active for ${resolvedDir} (sessionId: ${existing.sessionId}, status: ${existing.status})`
   125	      );
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    const client = new MockRpcClient({ cwd: resolvedDir, args: [] });
   129	    if (this.nextStartError) {
   130	      client.startError = this.nextStartError;
   131	      this.nextStartError = null;
   132	    }
   133	    if (this.nextInitError) {
   134	      client.initError = this.nextInitError;
   135	      this.nextInitError = null;
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    this.sessionCounter++;
   139	    client.initSessionId = `mock-session-${String(this.sessionCounter).padStart(3, '0')}`;
   140	    this.lastClient = client;
   141	    this.allClients.push(client);
   142	
   143	    // Create the session shell
   144	    const session: ManagedSession = {
   145	      sessionId: '',
   146	      projectDir: resolvedDir,
   147	      status: 'starting',
   148	      client: client as any, // duck-typed mock
   149	      events: [],
   150	      pendingBlocker: null,
   151	      cost: { totalCost: 0, tokens: { input: 0, output: 0, cacheRead: 0, cacheWrite: 0 } },
   152	      startTime: Date.now(),
   153	    };
   154	
   155	    // Insert into internal sessions map — access via protected method
   156	    this._putSession(resolvedDir, session);
   157	
   158	    try {
   159	      await client.start();
   160	
   161	      const initResult = await client.init();
   162	      session.sessionId = initResult.sessionId;
   163	      session.status = 'running';
   164	
   165	      // Wire event tracking using the same handleEvent logic as parent
   166	      session.unsubscribe = client.onEvent((event: Record<string, unknown>) => {
   167	        this._handleEvent(session, event);
   168	      });
   169	
   170	      // Kick off auto-mode
   171	      const command = options.command ?? '/gsd auto';
   172	      await client.prompt(command);
   173	
   174	      return session.sessionId;
   175	    } catch (err) {
   176	      session.status = 'error';
   177	      session.error = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   178	      try { await client.stop(); } catch { /* swallow */ }
   179	      throw new Error(`Failed to start session for ${resolvedDir}: ${session.error}`);
   180	    }
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  /** Expose internal session map insertion for testing */
   184	  _putSession(key: string, session: ManagedSession): void {
   185	    // Access the private sessions map via any cast
   186	    (this as any).sessions.set(key, session);
   187	  }
   188	
   189	  /** Expose handleEvent for testing */
   190	  _handleEvent(session: ManagedSession, event: Record<string, unknown>): void {
   191	    (this as any).handleEvent(session, event);
   192	  }
   193	}

   200	
   201	function createManager(): TestableSessionManager {
   202	  const mgr = new TestableSessionManager();
   203	  allManagers.push(mgr);
   204	  return mgr;

   267

   273	      (err: Error) => {

   275	        assert.ok(err.message.includes('spawn failed'));
   276	        return true;
   277	      },
   278	    );
   279	  });

   329	    const client = sm.lastClient!;
   330	
   331	    // Simulate a blocking UI request event
   332	    client.emitEvent({
   333	      type: 'extension_ui_request',
   334	      id: 'req-42',

   341	    assert.equal(session.status, 'blocked');

    11	function makeTmpBase(): string {
    12	  const base = join(tmpdir(), `gsd-mcp-workflow-${randomUUID()}`);
    13	  mkdirSync(join(base, ".gsd"), { recursive: true });
    14	  return base;
    15	}
    16	
    17	function cleanup(base: string): void {
    18	  try {
    19	    closeDatabase();
    20	  } catch {
    21	    // swallow
    22	  }
    23	  try {
    24	    rmSync(base, { recursive: true, force: true });
    25	  } catch {
    26	    // swallow
    27	  }
    28	}
    29	
    30	function writeWriteGateSnapshot(
    31	  base: string,
    32	  snapshot: { verifiedDepthMilestones?: string[]; activeQueuePhase?: boolean; pendingGateId?: string | null },
    33	): void {
    34	  mkdirSync(join(base, ".gsd", "runtime"), { recursive: true });
    35	  writeFileSync(
    36	    join(base, ".gsd", "runtime", "write-gate-state.json"),
    37	    JSON.stringify(
    38	      {
    39	        verifiedDepthMilestones: snapshot.verifiedDepthMilestones ?? [],
    40	        activeQueuePhase: snapshot.activeQueuePhase ?? false,
    41	        pendingGateId: snapshot.pendingGateId ?? null,
    42	      },
    43	      null,
    44	      2,
    45	    ),
    46	    "utf-8",
    47	  );
    48	}
    49	
    50	function makeMockServer() {
    51	  const tools: Array<{
    52	    name: string;
    53	    description: string;
    54	    params: Record<string, unknown>;
    55	    handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>;
    56	  }> = [];
    57	  return {
    58	    tools,
    59	    tool(
    60	      name: string,
    61	      description: string,
    62	      params: Record<string, unknown>,
    63	      handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>,
    64	    ) {
    65	      tools.push({ name, description, params, handler });
    66	    },
    67	  };
    68	}

2026-05-30 13:32:25,867 - INFO - swea-agent-gsd-build__gsd-2-3946 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

     * Creates an elicitation request for the given parameters.
     * For backwards compatibility, `mode` may be omitted for form requests and will default to `'form'`.
     * @param params The parameters for the elicitation request.
     * @param options Optional request options.
     * @returns The result of the elicitation request.
     */
    async elicitInput(params, options) {
        const mode = (params.mode ?? 'form');
        switch (mode) {
            case 'url': {
                if (!this._clientCapabilities?.elicitation?.url) {
                    throw new Error('Client does not support url elicitation.');
                }
                const urlParams = params;
                return this.request({ method: 'elicitation/create', params: urlParams }, types_js_1.ElicitResultSchema, options);
            }
            case 'form': {
                if (!this._clientCapabilities?.elicitation?.form) {
                    throw new Error('Client does not support form elicitation.');
                }
                const formParams = params.mode === 'form' ? params : { ...params, mode: 'form' };
                const result = await this.request({ method: 'elicitation/create', params: formParams }, types_js_1.ElicitResultSchema, options);
                if (result.action === 'accept' && result.content && formParams.requestedSchema) {
                    try {
                        const validator = this._jsonSchemaValidator.getValidator(formParams.requestedSchema);
                        const validationResult = validator(result.content);
                        if (!validationResult.valid) {
                            throw new types_js_1.McpError(types_js_1.ErrorCode.InvalidParams, `Elicitation response content does not match requested schema: ${validationResult.errorMessage}`);
                        }
                    }
                    catch (error) {
                        if (error instanceof types_js_1.McpError) {
                            throw error;
                        }
                        throw new types_js_1.McpError(types_js_1.ErrorCode.InternalError, `Error validating elicitation response: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`);
                    }
                }
                return result;
            }
        }
    }
    /**
     * Creates a reusable callback that, when invoked, will send a `notifications/elicitation/complete`
     * notification for the specified elicitation ID.
     *
     * @param elicitationId The ID of the elicitation to mark as complete.
     * @param options Optional notification options. Useful when the completion notification should be related to a prior request.
     * @returns A function that emits the completion notification when awaited.
     */
    createElicitationCompletionNotifier(elicitationId, options) {
        if (!this._clientCapabilities?.elicitation?.url) {
            throw new Error('Client does not support URL elicitation (required for notifications/elicitation/complete)');
        }

    71	  let current = resolve(startPath);
    72	
    73	  while (true) {
    74	    const candidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
    75	    if (existsSync(candidate)) return candidate;
    76	
    77	    const parent = dirname(current);
    78	    if (parent === current) break;
    79	    current = parent;
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  return null;
    83	}

   155	export function detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig(
   156	  projectRoot = process.cwd(),
   157	  env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = process.env,
   158	): WorkflowMcpLaunchConfig | null {
   159	  const name = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_NAME?.trim() || "gsd-workflow";
   160	  const explicitCommand = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_COMMAND?.trim();
   161	  const explicitArgs = parseJsonEnv<unknown>(env, "GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_ARGS");
   162	  const explicitEnv = parseJsonEnv<Record<string, string>>(env, "GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_ENV");
   163	  const explicitCwd = env.GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_CWD?.trim();
   164	  const gsdCliPath = env.GSD_CLI_PATH?.trim() || env.GSD_BIN_PATH?.trim();
   165	  const workflowProjectRoot =
   166	    explicitEnv?.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   167	    env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   168	    env.GSD_PROJECT_ROOT?.trim() ||
   169	    explicitCwd ||
   170	    projectRoot;
   171	  const resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot = resolve(workflowProjectRoot);
   172	
   173	  if (explicitCommand) {
   174	    const launchEnv = buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolve(workflowProjectRoot), gsdCliPath, explicitEnv);
   175	    return {
   176	      name,
   177	      command: explicitCommand,
   178	      args: Array.isArray(explicitArgs) && explicitArgs.length > 0 ? explicitArgs.map(String) : undefined,
   179	      cwd: explicitCwd || undefined,
   180	      env: Object.keys(launchEnv).length > 0 ? launchEnv : undefined,
   181	    };
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  const distCli = resolve(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
   185	  if (existsSync(distCli)) {
   186	    return {
   187	      name,
   188	      command: process.execPath,
   189	      args: [distCli],
   190	      cwd: resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot,
   191	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   192	    };
   193	  }
   194	
   195	  const bundledCli = getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env);
   196	  if (bundledCli) {
   197	    return {
   198	      name,
   199	      command: process.execPath,
   200	      args: [bundledCli],
   201	      cwd: resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot,
   202	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   203	    };
   204	  }
   205	
   206	  const binPath = lookupCommand("gsd-mcp-server");
   207	  if (binPath) {
   208	    return {
   209	      name,
   210	      command: binPath,
   211	      env: buildWorkflowLaunchEnv(resolvedWorkflowProjectRoot, gsdCliPath),
   212	    };
   213	  }
   214	
   215	  return null;

/**
 * Checks if an object is a Zod schema instance (v3 or v4).
 *
 * Zod schemas have internal markers:
 * - v3: `_def` property
 * - v4: `_zod` property
 *
 * This includes transformed schemas like z.preprocess(), z.transform(), z.pipe().
 */
function isZodSchemaInstance(obj) {
    return '_def' in obj || '_zod' in obj || isZodTypeLike(obj);
}
/**
 * Checks if an object is a "raw shape" - a plain object where values are Zod schemas.
 *
 * Raw shapes are used as shorthand: `{ name: z.string() }` instead of `z.object({ name: z.string() })`.
 *
 * IMPORTANT: This must NOT match actual Zod schema instances (like z.preprocess, z.pipe),
 * which have internal properties that could be mistaken for schema values.
 */
function isZodRawShapeCompat(obj) {
    if (typeof obj !== 'object' || obj === null) {
        return false;
    }
    // If it's already a Zod schema instance, it's NOT a raw shape
    if (isZodSchemaInstance(obj)) {
        return false;
    }
    // Empty objects are valid raw shapes (tools with no parameters)
    if (Object.keys(obj).length === 0) {
        return true;
    }
    // A raw shape has at least one property that is a Zod schema
    return Object.values(obj).some(isZodTypeLike);
}
/**
 * Converts a provided Zod schema to a Zod object if it is a ZodRawShapeCompat,
 * otherwise returns the schema as is.
 */
function getZodSchemaObject(schema) {
    if (!schema) {
        return undefined;
    }
    if (isZodRawShapeCompat(schema)) {
        return (0, zod_compat_js_1.objectFromShape)(schema);
    }
    return schema;
}
function promptArgumentsFromSchema(schema) {
    const shape = (0, zod_compat_js_1.getObjectShape)(schema);
    if (!shape)
        return [];
    return Object.entries(shape).map(([name, field]) => {
        // Get description - works for both v3 and v4
        const description = (0, zod_compat_js_1.getSchemaDescription)(field);
        // Check if optional - works for both v3 and v4
        const isOptional = (0, zod_compat_js_1.isSchemaOptional)(field);
        return {
            name,
            description,
            required: !isOptional
        };
    });
}
function getMethodValue(schema) {
    const shape = (0, zod_compat_js_1.getObjectShape)(schema);
    const methodSchema = shape?.method;
    if (!methodSchema) {
        throw new Error('Schema is missing a method literal');
    }
    // Extract literal value - works for both v3 and v4
    const value = (0, zod_compat_js_1.getLiteralValue)(methodSchema);
    if (typeof value === 'string') {
        return value;
    }
    throw new Error('Schema method literal must be a string');
}
function createCompletionResult(suggestions) {
    return {
        completion: {
            values: suggestions.slice(0, 100),
            total: suggestions.length,
            hasMore: suggestions.length > 100
        }
    };
}

    }

So the `Server` class has `elicitInput`. The `McpServer` wraps it and exposes `.server` to access the underlying `Server`. So I can do:

```typescript
const mcpServer = new McpServer(...);
// Now mcpServer.server.elicitInput(...) is available
```

Now let me design the `ask_user_questions` tool for the MCP server. It needs to:

1. Accept the same parameters as the in-process extension (questions with id, header, question, options, allowMultiple)
2. Use MCP form elicitation to present the questions
3. Return the same JSON answer shape

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/packages/mcp-server/src/server.ts   --old_str 'registerWorkflowTools(server);

  return { server };
}' --new_str '// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // ask_user_questions — structured user questions via MCP form elicitation
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  server.tool(
    '"'"'ask_user_questions'"'"',
    '"'"'Ask the user structured questions and wait for responses. Single-select questions have 2-3 mutually exclusive options with a free-form "None of the above" added automatically. Multi-select questions (allowMultiple: true) let the user toggle multiple options.'"'"',
    {
      questions: z.array(z.object({
        id: z.string().describe('"'"'Stable identifier for mapping answers (snake_case)'"'"'),
        header: z.string().describe('"'"'Short header label shown in the UI (12 or fewer chars)'"'"'),
        question: z.string().describe('"'"'Single-sentence prompt shown to the user'"'"'),
        options: z.array(z.object({
          label: z.string().describe('"'"'User-facing label (1-5 words)'"'"'),
          description: z.string().describe('"'"'One short sentence explaining impact/tradeoff if selected'"'"'),
        })).describe('"'"'Provide 2-3 mutually exclusive choices for single-select, or any number for multi-select. Put the recommended option first and suffix its label with "(Recommended)".'"'"'),
        allowMultiple: z.boolean().optional().describe('"'"'If true, the user can select multiple options. Default: false.'"'"'),
      })).describe('"'"'Questions to show the user. Prefer 1 and do not exceed 3.'"'"'),
    },
    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
      const { questions } = args as {
        questions: Array<{
          id: string;
          header: string;
          question: string;
          options: Array<{ label: string; description: string }>;
          allowMultiple?: boolean;
        }>;
      };

      if (!questions || questions.length === 0 || questions.length > 3) {
        return errorContent('"'"'ask_user_questions: questions must contain 1-3 items'"'"');
      }

      for (const q of questions) {
        if (!q.options || q.options.length === 0) {
          return errorContent(`ask_user_questions: question "${q.id}" has no options`);
        }
      }

      // Build form schema for MCP elicitation
      const formProperties: Record<string, unknown> = {};
      const requiredFields: string[] = [];

      for (const q of questions) {
        const multi = !!q.allowMultiple;
        const optionLabels = multi
          ? q.options.map((o) => o.label)
          : [...q.options.map((o) => o.label), '"'"'None of the above'"'"'];

        formProperties[q.id] = {
          type: multi ? '"'"'array'"'"' : '"'"'string'"'"',
          title: q.header,
          description: q.question,
          ...(multi
            ? {
                items: {
                  type: '"'"'string'"'"',
                  enum: optionLabels,
                },
                uniqueItems: true,
              }
            : {
                enum: optionLabels,
              }),
        };
        requiredFields.push(q.id);
      }

      const requestedSchema = {
        type: '"'"'object'"'"',
        properties: formProperties,
        required: requiredFields,
      };

      try {
        // Use MCP form elicitation (safe for non-secret structured choices).
        // secure_env_collect is NOT supported here — use URL elicitation for secrets.
        const result = await (server as any).server.elicitInput({
          message: '"'"'Please answer the following questions:'"'"',
          requestedSchema,
          mode: '"'"'form'"'"',
        });

        if (result.action !== '"'"'accept'"'"') {
          return jsonContent({ answers: {}, cancelled: true });
        }

        // Convert the form response to the GSD answer shape
        const answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> = {};
        const content = result.content as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
        if (content) {
          for (const q of questions) {
            const value = content[q.id];
            if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
              const list = Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value];
              answers[q.id] = { answers: list };
            } else {
              answers[q.id] = { answers: [] };
            }
          }
        }

        return jsonContent({ answers });
      } catch (err) {
        return errorContent(
          err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
        );
      }
    },
  );

  registerWorkflowTools(server);

  return { server };
}'

    // ask_user_questions — structured user questions via MCP form elicitation
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
    server.tool('"'"'ask_user_questions'"'"', '"'"'Ask the user structured questions and wait for responses. Single-select questions have 2-3 mutually exclusive options with a free-form "None of the above" added automatically. Multi-select questions (allowMultiple: true) let the user toggle multiple options.'"'"', {
        questions: z.array(z.object({
            id: z.string().describe('"'"'Stable identifier for mapping answers (snake_case)'"'"'),
            header: z.string().describe('"'"'Short header label shown in the UI (12 or fewer chars)'"'"'),
            question: z.string().describe('"'"'Single-sentence prompt shown to the user'"'"'),
            options: z.array(z.object({
                label: z.string().describe('"'"'User-facing label (1-5 words)'"'"'),
                description: z.string().describe('"'"'One short sentence explaining impact/tradeoff if selected'"'"'),
            })).describe('"'"'Provide 2-3 mutually exclusive choices for single-select, or any number for multi-select. Put the recommended option first and suffix its label with "(Recommended)".'"'"'),
            allowMultiple: z.boolean().optional().describe('"'"'If true, the user can select multiple options. Default: false.'"'"'),
        })).describe('"'"'Questions to show the user. Prefer 1 and do not exceed 3.'"'"'),
    }, async (args) => {
        const { questions } = args;
        if (!questions || questions.length === 0 || questions.length > 3) {
            return errorContent('"'"'ask_user_questions: questions must contain 1-3 items'"'"');
        }
        for (const q of questions) {
            if (!q.options || q.options.length === 0) {
                return errorContent(`ask_user_questions: question "${q.id}" has no options`);
            }
        }
        // Build form schema for MCP elicitation
        const formProperties = {};
        const requiredFields = [];
        for (const q of questions) {
            const multi = !!q.allowMultiple;
            const optionLabels = multi
                ? q.options.map((o) => o.label)
                : [...q.options.map((o) => o.label), '"'"'None of the above'"'"'];
            formProperties[q.id] = {
                type: multi ? '"'"'array'"'"' : '"'"'string'"'"',
                title: q.header,
                description: q.question,
                ...(multi
                    ? {
                        items: {
                            type: '"'"'string'"'"',
                            enum: optionLabels,
                        },
                        uniqueItems: true,
                    }
                    : {
                        enum: optionLabels,
                    }),
            };
            requiredFields.push(q.id);
        }
        const requestedSchema = {
            type: '"'"'object'"'"',
            properties: formProperties,
            required: requiredFields,
        };
        try {
            // Use MCP form elicitation (safe for non-secret structured choices).
            // secure_env_collect is NOT supported here — use URL elicitation for secrets.
            const result = await server.server.elicitInput({
                message: '"'"'Please answer the following questions:'"'"',
                requestedSchema,
                mode: '"'"'form'"'"',
            });
            if (result.action !== '"'"'accept'"'"') {
                return jsonContent({ answers: {}, cancelled: true });
            }
            // Convert the form response to the GSD answer shape
            const answers = {};
            const content = result.content;
            if (content) {
                for (const q of questions) {
                    const value = content[q.id];
                    if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
                        const list = Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value];
                        answers[q.id] = { answers: list };
                    }

                    }
                }

   322	            header: z.string().describe('Short header label shown in the UI (12 or fewer chars)'),
   323	            question: z.string().describe('Single-sentence prompt shown to the user'),
   324	            options: z.array(z.object({
   325	                label: z.string().describe('User-facing label (1-5 words)'),
   326	                description: z.string().describe('One short sentence explaining impact/tradeoff if selected'),
   327	            })).describe('Provide 2-3 mutually exclusive choices for single-select, or any number for multi-select. Put the recommended option first and suffix its label with "(Recommended)".'),
   328	            allowMultiple: z.boolean().optional().describe('If true, the user can select multiple options. Default: false.'),
   329	        })).describe('Questions to show the user. Prefer 1 and do not exceed 3.'),
   330	    }, async (args) => {
   331	        const { questions } = args;
   332	        if (!questions || questions.length === 0 || questions.length > 3) {
   333	            return errorContent('ask_user_questions: questions must contain 1-3 items');
   334	        }
   335	        for (const q of questions) {
   336	            if (!q.options || q.options.length === 0) {
   337	                return errorContent(`ask_user_questions: question "${q.id}" has no options`);
   338	            }
   339	        }
   340	        // Build form schema for MCP elicitation
   341	        const formProperties = {};
   342	        const requiredFields = [];
   343	        for (const q of questions) {
   344	            const multi = !!q.allowMultiple;
   345	            const optionLabels = multi
   346	                ? q.options.map((o) => o.label)
   347	                : [...q.options.map((o) => o.label), 'None of the above'];
   348	            formProperties[q.id] = {
   349	                type: multi ? 'array' : 'string',
   350	                title: q.header,
   351	                description: q.question,
   352	                ...(multi
   353	                    ? {
   354	                        items: {
   355	                            type: 'string',
   356	                            enum: optionLabels,
   357	                        },
   358	                        uniqueItems: true,
   359	                    }
   360	                    : {
   361	                        enum: optionLabels,
   362	                    }),
   363	            };
   364	            requiredFields.push(q.id);
   365	        }
   366	        const requestedSchema = {
   367	            type: 'object',
   368	            properties: formProperties,
   369	            required: requiredFields,
   370	        };
   371	        try {
   372	            // Use MCP form elicitation (safe for non-secret structured choices).
   373	            // secure_env_collect is NOT supported here — use URL elicitation for secrets.
   374	            const result = await server.server.elicitInput({
   375	                message: 'Please answer the following questions:',
   376	                requestedSchema,
   377	                mode: 'form',
   378	            });
   379	            if (result.action !== 'accept') {
   380	                return jsonContent({ answers: {}, cancelled: true });
   381	            }
   382	            // Convert the form response to the GSD answer shape
   383	            const answers = {};
   384	            const content = result.content;
   385	            if (content) {
   386	                for (const q of questions) {
   387	                    const value = content[q.id];
   388	                    if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
   389	                        const list = Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value];
   390	                        answers[q.id] = { answers: list };
   391	                    }
   392	                    else {
   393	                        answers[q.id] = { answers: [] };
   394	                    }
   395	                }
   396	            }
   397	            return jsonContent({ answers });
   398	        }
   399	        catch (err) {
   400	            return errorContent(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   401	        }
   402	    });
   403	    registerWorkflowTools(server);
   404	    return { server };
   405	}
   406	//# sourceMappingURL=server.js.map
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.

```ts
function getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv): string | null {
  ...
  const candidates = [
    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url))),

```

> make local workflow launches prefer live source modules and source CLI entrypoints when the TS resolve hook is available

I think this means: when we're running in a development environment where TypeScript source files can be directly executed (e.g., using `tsx` or `node --loader ts-node/esm`), we should prefer source files over dist files.

Now let me look at how the local workflow launch detection works. The key function is `detectWorkflowMcpLaunchConfig`. Currently:

1. It checks for an explicit command (`GSD_WORKFLOW_MCP_COMMAND`)
2. Then it checks for `packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js` 
3. Then it checks for bundled CLI path
4. Then it checks for `gsd-mcp-server` in PATH

The PR says: "make local workflow launches prefer live source modules and source CLI entrypoints when the TS resolve hook is available."

I think the change should be: when we detect that we're running in a development environment (e.g., the TS resolve hook is available), prefer source files. Let me check how to detect this.

Actually, looking at the `dev-cli.js` script, it imports `--import`, `resolve-ts.mjs`. The presence of the `--import` flag with resolve-ts can be detected by checking if `process.execArgv` contains something related. But a simpler approach: we can check if there's a `node_modules` with `tsx` or if the source files exist and `dist` files are stale.

Actually, let me re-read the PR description more carefully:

> In local checkout flows, the spawned workflow server could also drift behind source changes because the transport preferred stale dist artifacts.

The issue is that `findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath` prefers `dist/cli.js`. And `getBundledWorkflowExecutorModulePath` prefers `dist/resources/extensions/gsd/tools/workflow-tool-executors.js`. We should also look for the source files (`.ts`) and use them if available.

But wait - the MCP server is run as a separate process. You can't run `.ts` files directly without a TS runtime. So we need to either:
1. Use `tsx` or `node --loader` to run the TypeScript source
2. Or check if the source files are newer than dist files and use the source

I think the simpler approach is to check if we can use the source CLI (`packages/mcp-server/src/cli.ts`) with `tsx` or similar. Let me look at what the PR description suggests: "make local workflow launches prefer live source modules and source CLI entrypoints when the TS resolve hook is available."
