     9	export function resolve(specifier, context, nextResolve) {
    10	  // 1. Redirect all workspace package bare imports to source.
    11	  //    CI portability runs don't build any packages/ dist artifacts, so every
    12	  //    @gsd/* specifier (including transitive ones pulled in by pi-coding-agent
    13	  //    source itself) must resolve to the TypeScript source entrypoint.
    14	  if (specifier === "../../packages/pi-coding-agent/src/index.js") {
    15	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-coding-agent/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    16	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-coding-agent") {
    17	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-coding-agent/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    18	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-ai/oauth") {
    19	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-ai/src/utils/oauth/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    20	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-ai") {
    21	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-ai/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    22	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-agent-core") {
    23	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-agent-core/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    24	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/pi-tui") {
    25	    specifier = new URL("packages/pi-tui/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    26	  } else if (specifier === "@gsd/native") {
    27	    specifier = new URL("packages/native/src/index.ts", ROOT).href;
    28	  } else if (specifier.startsWith("@gsd/native/")) {
    29	    // Sub-path imports like @gsd/native/fd, @gsd/native/text, etc.
    30	    const subpath = specifier.slice("@gsd/native/".length);
    31	    specifier = new URL(`packages/native/src/${subpath}/index.ts`, ROOT).href;
    32	  }
    33	  // 2. Redirect packages/*/dist/ → packages/*/src/ with .js→.ts for strip-types
    34	  //    Also handles local imports — skip rewrite for dist/ paths that are real compiled artifacts.
    35	
    36	  else if (specifier.endsWith('.js') && (specifier.startsWith('./') || specifier.startsWith('../'))) {
    37	    if (context.parentURL && context.parentURL.includes('/src/')) {
    38	      if (specifier.includes('/dist/')) {
    39	        specifier = specifier.replace('/dist/', '/src/').replace(/\.js$/, '.ts');
    40	      } else {
    41	        specifier = specifier.replace(/\.js$/, '.ts');
    42	      }
    43	    }
    44	  }
    45	  // 3. Extensionless relative imports from web/ (Next.js convention).
    46	  //    Transpiled .tsx files emit extensionless imports — try .ts then .tsx.
    47	  else if (
    48	    (specifier.startsWith('./') || specifier.startsWith('../')) &&
    49	    !specifier.match(/\.\w+$/) &&
    50	    context.parentURL &&
    51	    context.parentURL.includes('/web/')
    52	  ) {
    53	    const baseUrl = new URL(specifier, context.parentURL);
    54	    for (const ext of ['.ts', '.tsx']) {
    55	      const candidate = fileURLToPath(baseUrl) + ext;
    56	      if (existsSync(candidate)) {
    57	        specifier = baseUrl.href + ext;
    58	        break;
    59	      }
    60	
    61	    }
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  return nextResolve(specifier, context);
    65	}
    66	
    67	export function load(url, context, nextLoad) {
    68	  // Node's --experimental-strip-types handles plain .ts but not .tsx and not
    69	  // all TypeScript syntax used by workspace packages (parameter properties,
    70	  // decorators, etc.). Transpile all workspace package source files and .tsx
    71	  // files through TypeScript's transpileModule to avoid those crashes.
    72	  const shouldTranspileWithTypeScript =
    73	    url.endsWith('.tsx') ||
    74	    (url.endsWith('.ts') && url.includes('/packages/') && url.includes('/src/'));
    75	
    76	  if (shouldTranspileWithTypeScript) {
    77	    const ts = require('typescript');
    78	    const source = readFileSync(fileURLToPath(url), 'utf-8');
    79	    const { outputText } = ts.transpileModule(source, {
    80	      fileName: fileURLToPath(url),
    81	      compilerOptions: {
    82	        jsx: ts.JsxEmit.ReactJSX,
    83	        module: ts.ModuleKind.ESNext,
    84	        target: ts.ScriptTarget.ESNext,
    85	        esModuleInterop: true,
    86	        experimentalDecorators: true,
    87	        emitDecoratorMetadata: true,
    88	      },
    89	    });
    90	    // Inject CJS-compatible globals (__dirname, __filename, require) so that
    91	    // workspace packages compiled as ESM can still use them.  This avoids the
    92	    // need for import.meta.url behind indirect invocation patterns that fail in
    93	    // CJS and in dynamically-created scopes.
    94	    // Only inject globals that the source file doesn't already declare itself.
    95	    const preambleLines = [
    96	      'import { fileURLToPath as __preamble_fUTP } from "node:url";',
    97	      'import { dirname as __preamble_dn } from "node:path";',
    98	      'import { createRequire as __preamble_cR } from "node:module";',
    99	    ];
   100	    if (!outputText.includes('const __filename') && !outputText.includes('let __filename')) {
   101	      preambleLines.push('const __filename = __preamble_fUTP(import.meta.url);');
   102	    }
   103	    if (!outputText.includes('const __dirname') && !outputText.includes('let __dirname')) {
   104	      preambleLines.push('const __dirname = __preamble_dn(__preamble_fUTP(import.meta.url));');
   105	    }
   106	    if (!outputText.includes('const require') && !outputText.includes('let require')) {
   107	      preambleLines.push('const require = __preamble_cR(import.meta.url);');
   108	    }
   109	    return { format: 'module', source: preambleLines.join('\n') + '\n' + outputText, shortCircuit: true };
   110	  }
   111	  return nextLoad(url, context);
   112	}

}' --new_str 'function findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(startPath) {
  let current = resolve(startPath);
  while (true) {
    // Prefer source CLI entrypoint when running from a checkout with the TS
    // resolve hook available so that local workflow launches stay aligned
    // with source changes instead of serving stale dist artifacts.
    const srcCandidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "src", "cli.ts");
    if (existsSync(srcCandidate)) return srcCandidate;
    const distCandidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
    if (existsSync(distCandidate)) return distCandidate;
    const parent = dirname(current);
    if (parent === current) break;
    current = parent;
  }
  return null;
}
function getBundledWorkflowMcpCliPath(env) {
  const envAnchors = [
    env.GSD_BIN_PATH?.trim(),
    env.GSD_CLI_PATH?.trim(),
    env.GSD_WORKFLOW_PATH?.trim()
  ].filter((value) => typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0);
  for (const anchor of envAnchors) {
    const candidate = findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(anchor);
    if (candidate) return candidate;
  }
  // Prefer source CLI entrypoint when running from a checkout so that
  // local workflow launches stay aligned with source changes instead of
  // serving stale dist artifacts.
  const candidates = [
    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../packages/mcp-server/src/cli.ts", import.meta.url))),
    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url))),
    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../../packages/mcp-server/src/cli.ts", import.meta.url))),
    resolve(fileURLToPath(new URL("../../../../../packages/mcp-server/dist/cli.js", import.meta.url)))
  ];
  for (const bundledCli of candidates) {
    if (existsSync(bundledCli)) return bundledCli;
  }
  return null;
}

    46	function findWorkflowCliFromAncestorPath(startPath) {
    47	  let current = resolve(startPath);
    48	  while (true) {
    49	    // Prefer source CLI entrypoint when running from a checkout with the TS
    50	    // resolve hook available so that local workflow launches stay aligned
    51	    // with source changes instead of serving stale dist artifacts.
    52	    const srcCandidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "src", "cli.ts");
    53	    if (existsSync(srcCandidate)) return srcCandidate;
    54	    const distCandidate = resolve(current, "packages", "mcp-server", "dist", "cli.js");
    55	    if (existsSync(distCandidate)) return distCandidate;
    56	    const parent = dirname(current);
    57	    if (parent === current) break;
    58	    current = parent;
    59	  }
    60	  return null;
    61	}

@@ -407,6 +407,117 @@ export async function createMcpServer(sessionManager: SessionManager): Promise<{
     },
   );
 
+  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+  // ask_user_questions — structured user questions via MCP form elicitation
+  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+  server.tool(
+    'ask_user_questions',
+    'Ask the user structured questions and wait for responses. Single-select questions have 2-3 mutually exclusive options with a free-form "None of the above" added automatically. Multi-select questions (allowMultiple: true) let the user toggle multiple options.',
+    {
+      questions: z.array(z.object({
+        id: z.string().describe('Stable identifier for mapping answers (snake_case)'),
+        header: z.string().describe('Short header label shown in the UI (12 or fewer chars)'),
+        question: z.string().describe('Single-sentence prompt shown to the user'),
+        options: z.array(z.object({
+          label: z.string().describe('User-facing label (1-5 words)'),
+          description: z.string().describe('One short sentence explaining impact/tradeoff if selected'),
+        })).describe('Provide 2-3 mutually exclusive choices for single-select, or any number for multi-select. Put the recommended option first and suffix its label with "(Recommended)".'),
+        allowMultiple: z.boolean().optional().describe('If true, the user can select multiple options. Default: false.'),
+      })).describe('Questions to show the user. Prefer 1 and do not exceed 3.'),
+    },
+    async (args: Record<string, unknown>) => {
+      const { questions } = args as {
+        questions: Array<{
+          id: string;
+          header: string;
+          question: string;
+          options: Array<{ label: string; description: string }>;
+          allowMultiple?: boolean;
+        }>;
+      };
+
+      if (!questions || questions.length === 0 || questions.length > 3) {
+        return errorContent('ask_user_questions: questions must contain 1-3 items');
+      }
+
+      for (const q of questions) {
+        if (!q.options || q.options.length === 0) {
+          return errorContent(`ask_user_questions: question "${q.id}" has no options`);
+        }
+      }
+
+      // Build form schema for MCP elicitation
+      const formProperties: Record<string, unknown> = {};
+      const requiredFields: string[] = [];
+
+      for (const q of questions) {
+        const multi = !!q.allowMultiple;
+        const optionLabels = multi
+          ? q.options.map((o) => o.label)
+          : [...q.options.map((o) => o.label), 'None of the above'];
+
+        formProperties[q.id] = {
+          type: multi ? 'array' : 'string',
+          title: q.header,
+          description: q.question,
+          ...(multi
+            ? {
+                items: {
+                  type: 'string',
+                  enum: optionLabels,
+                },
+                uniqueItems: true,
+              }
+            : {
+                enum: optionLabels,
+              }),
+        };
+        requiredFields.push(q.id);
+      }
+
+      const requestedSchema = {
+        type: 'object',
+        properties: formProperties,
+        required: requiredFields,
+      };
+
+      try {
+        // Use MCP form elicitation (safe for non-secret structured choices).
+        // secure_env_collect is NOT supported here — use URL elicitation for secrets.
+        const result = await (server as any).server.elicitInput({
+          message: 'Please answer the following questions:',
+          requestedSchema,
+          mode: 'form',
+        });
+
+        if (result.action !== 'accept') {
+          return jsonContent({ answers: {}, cancelled: true });
+        }
+
+        // Convert the form response to the GSD answer shape
+        const answers: Record<string, { answers: string[] }> = {};
+        const content = result.content as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
+        if (content) {
+          for (const q of questions) {
+            const value = content[q.id];
+            if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
+              const list = Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value];
+              answers[q.id] = { answers: list };
+            } else {
+              answers[q.id] = { answers: [] };
+            }
+          }
+        }
+
+        return jsonContent({ answers });
+      } catch (err) {
+        return errorContent(
+          err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
+        );
+      }
+    },
+  );
+
   registerWorkflowTools(server);
 
   return { server };
